Experimental results on four benchmarks show that MAPLE consistently and significantly outperforms existing TTRL methods and standalone reward model selection, demonstrating that structured process rewards are key for reliable and scalable medical AI.
本文针对医学推理中标准测试时强化学习方法依赖不可靠多数投票进行监督的局限性，提出了MAPLE这一统一训练范式。该方法将医学过程奖励模型与测试时强化学习相结合，用专家对齐的逐步监督替代多数投票，从而依据医学正确性而非统计共识来指导强化学习。在四个基准测试上的广泛评估表明，MAPLE方法持续且显著地优于现有的测试时强化学习及独立奖励模型选择方法，证明从随机启发式转向结构化、逐步的奖励对于开发可靠、可扩展的医疗AI系统至关重要。
A Survey of Reinforcement Learning For Economics
Authors: Pranjal Rawat
First: 2026-03-09T21:43:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T21:43:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This survey (re)introduces reinforcement learning methods to economists. The curse of dimensionality limits how far exact dynamic programming can be effectively applied, forcing us to rely on suitably "small" problems or our ability to convert "big" problems into smaller ones. While this reduction has been sufficient for many classical applications, a growing class of economic models resists such reduction. Reinforcement learning algorithms offer a natural, sample-based extension of dynamic programming, extending tractability to problems with high-dimensional states, continuous actions, and strategic interactions. I review the theory connecting classical planning to modern learning algorithms and demonstrate their mechanics through simulated examples in pricing, inventory control, strategic games, and preference elicitation. I also examine the practical vulnerabilities of these algorithms, noting their brittleness, sample inefficiency, sensitivity to hyperparameters, and the absence of global convergence guarantees outside of tabular settings. The successes of reinforcement learning remain strictly bounded by these constraints, as well as a reliance on accurate simulators. When guided by economic structure, reinforcement learning provides a remarkably flexible framework. It stands as an imperfect, but promising, addition to the computational economist's toolkit. A companion survey (Rust and Rawat, 2026b) covers the inverse problem of inferring preferences from observed behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习在经济学中的应用综述
本综述（重新）向经济学家介绍强化学习方法。维度灾难限制了精确动态规划的有效应用范围，迫使我们依赖适当的“小”问题或将“大”问题转化为较小问题的能力。虽然这种简化对许多经典应用已足够，但日益增长的经济模型类别抵制此类简化。强化学习算法提供了一种自然的、基于样本的动态规划扩展，将可处理性延伸至高维状态、连续动作和策略交互的问题。我回顾了连接经典规划与现代学习算法的理论，并通过定价、库存控制、策略博弈和偏好诱导的模拟示例展示其机制。同时，我审视了这些算法的实际脆弱性，指出其脆弱性、样本效率低下、对超参数的敏感性，以及在表格设定外缺乏全局收敛保证。强化学习的成功仍严格受限于这些约束，以及对精确模拟器的依赖。当以经济结构为指导时，强化学习提供了一个极其灵活的框架。它虽不完美，但有望成为计算经济学家工具包中的补充。配套综述（Rust and Rawat, 2026b）涵盖了从观测行为推断偏好的逆问题。
Summary / 总结
This survey reintroduces reinforcement learning (RL) to economists, motivated by the limitations of exact dynamic programming which struggles with high-dimensional economic models that resist simplification. The method involves using RL algorithms as a sample-based extension of dynamic programming to handle problems with complex states, continuous actions, and strategic interactions. Experimental demonstrations in simulated examples like pricing and inventory control show RL's flexibility, but results also reveal practical vulnerabilities including brittleness, sample inefficiency, and sensitivity to hyperparameters, highlighting that its success remains bounded by these constraints and a reliance on accurate simulators.
本调查向经济学家重新介绍了强化学习方法，其动机在于精确动态规划受限于维数诅咒，难以处理无法简化的高维经济模型。该方法将强化学习算法作为动态规划的样本扩展，以应对具有复杂状态、连续动作和策略互动的问题。在定价和库存控制等模拟示例中的实验演示表明强化学习具有灵活性，但结果也揭示了其实际脆弱性，包括脆弱性、样本效率低下和对超参数的敏感性，强调其成功仍受这些限制以及对精确模拟器的依赖所约束。
Interpretable Markov-Based Spatiotemporal Risk Surfaces for Missing-Child Search Planning with Reinforcement Learning and LLM-Based Quality Assurance
Authors: Joshua Castillo, Ravi Mukkamala
First: 2026-03-09T21:08:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T21:08:29+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 7 figures. Accepted at ICEIS 2026 (International Conference on Enterprise Information Systems)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The first 72 hours of a missing-child investigation are critical for successful recovery. However, law enforcement agencies often face fragmented, unstructured data and a lack of dynamic, geospatial predictive tools. Our system, Guardian, provides an end-to-end decision-support system for missing-child investigation and early search planning. It converts heterogeneous, unstructured case documents into a schema-aligned spatiotemporal representation, enriches cases with geocoding and transportation context, and provides probabilistic search products spanning 0-72 hours. In this paper, we present an overview of Guardian as well as a detailed description of a three-layer predictive component of the system. The first layer is a Markov chain, a sparse, interpretable model with transitions incorporating road accessibility costs, seclusion preferences, and corridor bias with separate day/night parameterizations. The Markov chain's output prediction distributions are then transformed into operationally useful search plans by the second layer's reinforcement learning. Finally, the third layer's LLM performs post hoc validation of layer 2 search plans prior to their release. Using a synthetic but realistic case study, we report quantitative outputs across 24/48/72-hour horizons and analyze sensitivity, failure modes, and tradeoffs. Results show that the proposed predictive system with the three-layer architecture produces interpretable priors for zone optimization and human review.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于可解释马尔可夫链的时空风险面：结合强化学习与LLM质量保障的失踪儿童搜寻规划系统
失踪儿童案件的前72小时是成功找回的关键窗口，但执法机构常面临数据碎片化、非结构化及缺乏动态地理空间预测工具的困境。本系统'守护者'提供端到端的失踪儿童调查与早期搜寻决策支持：将异构非结构化案件文档转换为模式对齐的时空表征，通过地理编码与交通情境增强案件信息，并生成覆盖0-72小时的概率化搜寻产品。本文系统阐述守护者架构，并重点解析其三层次预测组件：第一层采用马尔可夫链构建稀疏可解释模型，其状态转移融合道路通达成本、隐蔽偏好与通道偏向因子，并区分昼夜参数化；第二层通过强化学习将马尔可夫链输出的概率分布转化为可操作的搜寻方案；第三层利用大语言模型对第二层方案进行发布前事后验证。基于合成但贴近现实的案例研究，我们展示了24/48/72小时时间跨度的量化输出，并系统分析敏感性、失效模式与权衡关系。结果表明，该三层次预测架构能为区域优化与人工复核提供可解释的先验概率框架。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the critical first 72 hours in missing-child cases and the lack of dynamic geospatial tools for law enforcement, this paper introduces Guardian, an end-to-end decision-support system. The method involves a three-layer predictive component: first, an interpretable Markov chain model incorporating road accessibility and temporal biases generates spatiotemporal risk distributions; second, reinforcement learning transforms these into operational search plans; third, a large language model (LLM) performs post hoc validation. Experimental results from a realistic synthetic case study demonstrate that the system produces quantitatively assessed, interpretable priors for search zone optimization across 24, 48, and 72-hour horizons, enabling effective human review.
本研究针对儿童失踪案件关键的黄金72小时以及执法部门缺乏动态地理空间预测工具的现状，提出了名为Guardian的端到端决策支持系统。其方法采用三层预测架构：首先，一个融合道路可达性、隐蔽偏好和昼夜差异的可解释马尔可夫链模型生成时空风险分布；其次，通过强化学习将这些分布转化为可操作的搜救计划；最后，利用大语言模型（LLM）对计划进行事后验证。基于合成但真实的案例实验表明，该系统能够在24、48和72小时的时间跨度内，为搜救区域优化生成可量化评估、可解释的先验概率，以支持有效的人工审核。
Optimizing Reinforcement Learning Training over Digital Twin Enabled Multi-fidelity Networks
Authors: Hanzhi Yu, Hasan Farooq, Julien Forgeat, Shruti Bothe, Kristijonas Cyras, Md Moin Uddin Chowdhury, Mingzhe Chen
First: 2026-03-09T20:59:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T20:59:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we investigate a novel digital network twin (DNT) assisted deep learning (DL) model training framework. In particular, we consider a physical network where a base station (BS) uses several antennas to serve multiple mobile users, and a DNT that is a virtual representation of the physical network. The BS must adjust its antenna tilt angles to optimize the data rates of all users. Due to user mobility, the BS may not be able to accurately track network dynamics such as wireless channels and user mobilities. Hence, a reinforcement learning (RL) approach is used to dynamically adjust the antenna tilt angles. To train the RL, we can use data collected from the physical network and the DNT. The data collected from the physical network is more accurate but incurs more communication overhead compared to the data collected from the DNT. Therefore, it is necessary to determine the ratio of data collected from the physical network and the DNT to improve the training of the RL model. We formulate this problem as an optimization problem whose goal is to jointly optimize the tilt angle adjustment policy and the data collection strategy, aiming to maximize the data rates of all users while constraining the time delay introduced by collecting data from the physical network. To solve this problem, we propose a hierarchical RL framework that integrates robust adversarial loss and proximal policy optimization (PPO). Simulation results show that our proposed method reduces the physical network data collection delay by up to 28.01% and 1x compared to a hierarchical RL that uses vanilla PPO as the first level RL, and the baseline that uses robust-RL at the first level and selects the data collection ratio randomly.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于数字孪生多保真度网络的强化学习训练优化
本文研究了一种新型数字网络孪生辅助的深度学习模型训练框架。具体而言，我们考虑一个物理网络，其中基站通过多天线服务多个移动用户，同时存在一个作为物理网络虚拟映射的数字网络孪生。基站需调整天线倾角以优化所有用户的数据速率。由于用户移动性，基站可能无法精确跟踪无线信道与用户移动等网络动态，因此采用强化学习方法动态调整天线倾角。为训练强化学习模型，可同时使用物理网络与数字网络孪生采集的数据：物理网络数据精度更高但通信开销更大，故需确定二者数据采集比例以优化模型训练。我们将该问题建模为联合优化倾角调整策略与数据采集策略的优化问题，目标是在约束物理网络数据采集时延的前提下最大化用户数据速率。为此，提出一种融合鲁棒对抗损失与近端策略优化的分层强化学习框架。仿真结果表明：相较于采用标准近端策略优化的分层强化学习方法，以及首层采用鲁棒强化学习并随机选择数据采集比例的基线方法，所提方法将物理网络数据采集时延降低了最高达28.01%与1倍。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the challenge of optimizing antenna tilt angles in a mobile network using reinforcement learning (RL), where accurate real-world data collection incurs high communication overhead. The proposed method introduces a digital network twin (DNT) to provide simulated data, formulating an optimization problem to jointly learn the tilt adjustment policy and the data collection strategy from both physical and virtual sources via a hierarchical RL framework integrating robust adversarial loss and proximal policy optimization (PPO). Experimental simulations demonstrate that this approach reduces physical network data collection delay by up to 28.01% and outperforms baseline hierarchical RL and random strategy methods in maximizing user data rates.
本文针对移动网络中利用强化学习优化天线倾角时，真实数据收集通信开销高的问题，提出一种数字网络孪生辅助的训练框架。该方法通过数字孪生提供仿真数据，将倾角调整策略与虚实数据收集比例联合优化，设计了一个结合鲁棒对抗损失和近端策略优化的分层强化学习算法。仿真结果表明，所提方法能减少高达28.01%的物理网络数据收集延迟，在提升用户数据速率方面优于基准分层强化学习和随机策略。
APPLV: Adaptive Planner Parameter Learning from Vision-Language-Action Model
Authors: Yuanjie Lu, Beichen Wang, Zhengqi Wu, Yang Li, Xiaomin Lin, Chengzhi Mao, Xuesu Xiao
First: 2026-03-09T19:23:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T19:23:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous navigation in highly constrained environments remains challenging for mobile robots. Classical navigation approaches offer safety assurances but require environment-specific parameter tuning; end-to-end learning bypasses parameter tuning but struggles with precise control in constrained spaces. To this end, recent robot learning approaches automate parameter tuning while retaining classical systems' safety, yet still face challenges in generalizing to unseen environments. Recently, Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown promise by leveraging foundation models' scene understanding capabilities, but still struggle with precise control and inference latency in navigation tasks. In this paper, we propose Adaptive Planner Parameter Learning from Vision-Language-Action Model (\textsc{applv}). Unlike traditional VLA models that directly output actions, \textsc{applv} leverages pre-trained vision-language models with a regression head to predict planner parameters that configure classical planners. We develop two training strategies: supervised learning fine-tuning from collected navigation trajectories and reinforcement learning fine-tuning to further optimize navigation performance. We evaluate \textsc{applv} across multiple motion planners on the simulated Benchmark Autonomous Robot Navigation (BARN) dataset and in physical robot experiments. Results demonstrate that \textsc{applv} outperforms existing methods in both navigation performance and generalization to unseen environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：APPLV：基于视觉-语言-动作模型的自适应规划器参数学习
在高度受限环境中实现自主导航对移动机器人仍具挑战性。经典导航方法虽能提供安全保障，但需针对特定环境调整参数；端到端学习虽免去参数调优，却在受限空间中难以实现精确控制。为此，近期机器人学习方法在保持经典系统安全性的同时实现了参数自动调优，但仍面临泛化至未知环境的难题。视觉-语言-动作模型通过利用基础模型的场景理解能力展现出潜力，但在导航任务中仍受限于精确控制与推理延迟。本文提出基于视觉-语言-动作模型的自适应规划器参数学习方法。与传统直接输出动作的VLA模型不同，该方法通过预训练视觉-语言模型配合回归头预测规划器参数，以配置经典规划器。我们开发了两种训练策略：基于采集导航轨迹的监督学习微调，以及进一步优化导航性能的强化学习微调。我们在仿真BARN数据集与实体机器人实验中，通过多种运动规划器对方法进行评估。结果表明，该方法在导航性能与未知环境泛化能力上均优于现有方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of autonomous robot navigation in constrained environments, where classical planners require manual parameter tuning and end-to-end learning lacks precision. The proposed method, APPLV, adapts a Vision-Language-Action model to predict parameters for classical planners instead of direct actions, using supervised and reinforcement learning for fine-tuning. Experimental results on the BARN dataset and physical robots show improved navigation performance and better generalization to unseen environments compared to existing approaches.
本文针对受限环境中自主机器人导航的挑战，即传统规划器需手动调整参数而端到端学习缺乏精确性的问题，提出了APPLV方法。该方法利用视觉-语言-动作模型预测传统规划器的参数而非直接输出动作，并通过监督学习和强化学习进行微调。在BARN数据集和实体机器人上的实验结果表明，该方法在导航性能和未见过环境的泛化能力上均优于现有方法。
Bradley-Terry Policy Optimization for Generative Preference Modeling
Authors: Shengyu Feng, Yun He, Shuang Ma, Beibin Li, Yuanhao Xiong, Songlin Li, Karishma Mandyam, Julian Katz-Samuels, Shengjie Bi, Licheng Yu, Hejia Zhang, Karthik Abinav Sankararaman, Han Fang, Yiming Yang, Manaal Faruqui
First: 2025-10-17T02:14:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T19:10:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has recently proven effective at scaling chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning in large language models for tasks with verifiable answers. However, extending RL-based thought training to more general non-verifiable tasks-where supervision is provided only through pairwise human preferences-remains challenging. Existing approaches typically apply RL objectives designed for verifiable rewards to preference-based settings in a heuristic manner. In this work, we show that introducing CoT reasoning into preference modeling fundamentally changes the structure of the Bradley-Terry (BT) likelihood, as the reasoning process must be treated as a latent variable. This results in a preference likelihood expressed as a ratio of expectations over stochastic generation trajectories, which cannot be optimized using Jensen-style bounds or standard RL objectives. To address this challenge, we derive a consistent Monte Carlo estimator for the gradient of the resulting likelihood, leading to Bradley-Terry Policy Optimization (BTPO). Empirically, BTPO enables stable and effective training of generative preference models with CoT reasoning, consistently outperforming prior heuristic approaches across multiple benchmarks and model scales.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向生成式偏好建模的布拉德利-特里策略优化
强化学习近期被证明能有效扩展大语言模型的思维链推理能力，适用于答案可验证的任务。然而，将基于强化学习的思维训练推广至更广泛的不可验证任务——仅通过成对人类偏好提供监督——仍具挑战。现有方法通常将以可验证奖励设计的强化学习目标启发式地应用于偏好场景。本研究表明，将思维链推理引入偏好建模会从根本上改变布拉德利-特里似然函数的结构，因为推理过程必须被视为潜变量。这导致偏好似然需表达为随机生成轨迹的期望比值，无法通过詹森型边界或标准强化学习目标进行优化。为解决该问题，我们推导出对应似然函数梯度的一致蒙特卡洛估计量，从而提出布拉德利-特里策略优化方法。实证表明，该方法能稳定有效地训练具备思维链推理的生成式偏好模型，在多个基准测试和模型规模上持续优于先前的启发式方法。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to extend reinforcement learning-based training of chain-of-thought reasoning from tasks with verifiable answers to more general non-verifiable tasks supervised only by pairwise human preferences, which remains challenging as existing methods apply RL objectives heuristically. The method introduces Bradley-Terry Policy Optimization (BTPO), a novel approach derived by treating reasoning as a latent variable in the Bradley-Terry likelihood, which results in a preference likelihood expressed as a ratio of expectations over stochastic trajectories, and it provides a consistent Monte Carlo estimator for gradient optimization. The main experimental results show that BTPO enables stable and effective training of generative preference models with chain-of-thought reasoning, consistently outperforming prior heuristic approaches across multiple benchmarks and model scales.
本研究的动机是将基于强化学习的思维链推理训练从答案可验证的任务扩展到仅通过成对人类偏好监督的更一般的不可验证任务，这具有挑战性，因为现有方法以启发式方式应用强化学习目标。该方法提出了布拉德利-特里策略优化，通过将推理视为布拉德利-特里似然中的隐变量，推导出一种新颖方法，导致偏好似然表示为随机轨迹上的期望比率，并提供了用于梯度优化的一致蒙特卡洛估计器。主要实验结果表明，该方法能稳定有效地训练具有思维链推理的生成式偏好模型，在多个基准测试和模型规模上持续优于先前的启发式方法。
Small Language Models for Efficient Agentic Tool Calling: Outperforming Large Models with Targeted Fine-tuning
Authors: Polaris Jhandi, Owais Kazi, Shreyas Subramanian, Neel Sendas
Venue: AAAI 2026
First: 2025-12-17T20:12:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T18:40:10+00:00
Comments: Accepted at AAAI 2026 Workshop on Agentic AI Benchmarks and Applications for Enterprise Tasks
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As organizations scale adoption of generative AI, model cost optimization and operational efficiency have emerged as critical factors determining sustainability and accessibility. While Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate impressive capabilities across diverse tasks, their extensive computational requirements make them cost-prohibitive for routine enterprise use. This limitation motivates the exploration of Small Language Models (SLMs), which can deliver comparable performance in targeted applications while drastically reducing infrastructure overhead (Irugalbandara et al., 2023). In this work, we investigate the feasibility of replacing LLM-driven workflows with optimized SLMs. We trained a domain-adapted SLM to execute representative tasks traditionally handled by LLMs, such as document summarization, query answering, and structured data interpretation. As part of the experiment, we investigated the fine-tuning of facebook/opt-350m model (single epoch only) using the Hugging Face TRL (Transformer Reinforcement Learning), specifically the Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) trainer. The OPT-350M model was released by Meta AI in 2022 as part of the OPT (Open Pretrained Transformer) family of models. Similar studies demonstrate that even models at the 350M parameter scale can meaningfully contribute to instruction-tuning pipelines (Mekala et al., 2024). Experimental results demonstrated that our fine-tuned SLM achieves exceptional performance with a 77.55\% pass rate on ToolBench evaluation, significantly outperforming all baseline models including ChatGPT-CoT (26.00\%), ToolLLaMA-DFS (30.18\%), and ToolLLaMA-CoT (16.27\%). These findings emphasize that thoughtful design and targeted training of SLMs can significantly lower barriers to adoption, enabling cost-effective, large-scale integration of generative AI into production systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：高效代理工具调用的小型语言模型：通过定向微调超越大型模型
随着各组织规模化采用生成式AI，模型成本优化与运行效率已成为决定可持续性与可及性的关键因素。尽管大型语言模型（LLM）在多样化任务中展现出卓越能力，但其庞大的计算需求使其在企业常规应用中成本过高。这一局限性推动了对小型语言模型（SLM）的探索——后者能在定向应用中提供相当性能，同时大幅降低基础设施开销（Irugalbandara等人，2023）。本研究探讨了用优化SLM替代LLM驱动工作流的可行性。我们训练了一个领域适配的SLM来执行传统由LLM处理的代表性任务，如文档摘要、查询应答和结构化数据解析。实验中，我们使用Hugging Face TRL（Transformer强化学习）框架中的监督微调（SFT）训练器，对facebook/opt-350m模型进行了单轮微调。OPT-350M模型由Meta AI于2022年作为OPT（开放预训练Transformer）系列发布。同类研究表明，即使是3.5亿参数规模的模型也能对指令微调流程产生实质性贡献（Mekala等人，2024）。实验结果显示，我们微调后的SLM在ToolBench评估中以77.55%的通过率取得卓越性能，显著超越所有基线模型（包括ChatGPT-CoT的26.00%、ToolLLaMA-DFS的30.18%和ToolLLaMA-CoT的16.27%）。这些发现强调，通过精心设计和定向训练，SLM能显著降低应用门槛，实现生成式AI在经济高效的大规模生产系统集成。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to reduce the high computational costs of large language models (LLMs) for sustainable enterprise AI adoption, this work explores whether small language models (SLMs) can effectively replace LLMs in agentic tool-calling tasks. The method involves targeted fine-tuning of the OPT-350M model using supervised fine-tuning (SFT) via the Hugging Face TRL library to handle tasks like document summarization and structured data interpretation. The main experimental result shows the fine-tuned SLM achieved a 77.55% pass rate on the ToolBench evaluation, substantially outperforming baseline models including ChatGPT-CoT (26.00%) and ToolLLaMA variants, demonstrating that optimized SLMs can offer a cost-efficient alternative to LLMs for specific workflows.
本研究旨在解决大型语言模型（LLM）计算成本高昂的问题，以促进生成式AI在企业中的可持续应用，探索了小型语言模型（SLM）在代理工具调用任务中替代LLM的可行性。方法上，通过Hugging Face TRL库的监督微调（SFT）对OPT-350M模型进行针对性微调，使其能够执行文档摘要和结构化数据解释等任务。主要实验结果表明，微调后的SLM在ToolBench评估中达到了77.55%的通过率，显著优于ChatGPT-CoT（26.00%）和ToolLLaMA等基线模型，证明经过优化的SLM在特定工作流中可以成为LLM的高性价比替代方案。
Multi-level meta-reinforcement learning with skill-based curriculum
Authors: Sichen Yang, Mauro Maggioni
First: 2026-03-09T17:59:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T17:59:39+00:00
Comments: 78 pages, 12 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider problems in sequential decision making with natural multi-level structure, where sub-tasks are assembled together to accomplish complex goals. Systematically inferring and leveraging hierarchical structure has remained a longstanding challenge; we describe an efficient multi-level procedure for repeatedly compressing Markov decision processes (MDPs), wherein a parametric family of policies at one level is treated as single actions in the compressed MDPs at higher levels, while preserving the semantic meanings and structure of the original MDP, and mimicking the natural logic to address a complex MDP. Higher-level MDPs are themselves independent MDPs with less stochasticity, and may be solved using existing algorithms. As a byproduct, spatial or temporal scales may be coarsened at higher levels, making it more efficient to find long-term optimal policies. The multi-level representation delivered by this procedure decouples sub-tasks from each other and usually greatly reduces unnecessary stochasticity and the policy search space, leading to fewer iterations and computations when solving the MDPs. A second fundamental aspect of this work is that these multi-level decompositions plus the factorization of policies into embeddings (problem-specific) and skills (including higher-order functions) yield new transfer opportunities of skills across different problems and different levels. This whole process is framed within curriculum learning, wherein a teacher organizes the student agent's learning process in a way that gradually increases the difficulty of tasks and and promotes transfer across MDPs and levels within and across curricula. The consistency of this framework and its benefits can be guaranteed under mild assumptions. We demonstrate abstraction, transferability, and curriculum learning in examples, including MazeBase+, a more complex variant of the MazeBase example.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于技能课程的多层次元强化学习
我们研究具有自然多层次结构的序列决策问题，其中子任务被组合以实现复杂目标。系统性地推断并利用层次结构一直是一个长期挑战；我们提出一种高效的多层次过程，用于重复压缩马尔可夫决策过程（MDPs）。在该过程中，某一层次的参数化策略族在更高层次的压缩MDP中被视为单一动作，同时保留原始MDP的语义含义与结构，并模拟自然逻辑以处理复杂MDP。更高层次的MDP本身是随机性更低的独立MDP，可用现有算法求解。作为副产品，空间或时间尺度可在更高层次被粗化，从而更高效地寻找长期最优策略。此过程产生的多层次表征使子任务相互解耦，通常能大幅减少不必要的随机性和策略搜索空间，从而在求解MDP时减少迭代与计算量。本工作的第二个核心在于：这些多层次分解加上将策略因子化为嵌入（问题特定）与技能（包括高阶函数），为技能在不同问题及不同层次间创造了新的迁移机会。整个过程置于课程学习框架中，教师通过逐步提升任务难度、促进MDP间及课程内外的跨层次迁移来组织智能体的学习过程。该框架的一致性及其优势在温和假设下可得到保证。我们在包括MazeBase+（MazeBase示例的复杂变体）等案例中展示了抽象化、可迁移性与课程学习的效果。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of leveraging hierarchical structure in complex sequential decision-making tasks, where sub-tasks combine to achieve overarching goals. The method introduces a multi-level procedure that compresses Markov decision processes (MDPs) by treating lower-level policy families as single actions in higher-level MDPs, preserving semantic structure and reducing stochasticity and policy search space. Experimental results, including tests on MazeBase+, demonstrate that this approach enables efficient abstraction, skill transfer across problems and levels, and effective curriculum learning, leading to fewer iterations and computations while guaranteeing benefits under mild assumptions.
该论文针对具有自然多层次结构的顺序决策问题，旨在利用层次结构解决子任务组合实现复杂目标的挑战。方法提出一种多层次过程，通过将低层策略族压缩为高层马尔可夫决策过程中的单动作，保留原始语义结构并减少随机性和策略搜索空间。实验结果表明，在包括MazeBase+等示例中，该方法实现了高效的抽象、跨问题和跨层次的技能迁移以及课程学习，从而减少了迭代和计算量，并在温和假设下保证了其益处。
Agentic Critical Training
Authors: Weize Liu, Minghui Liu, Sy-Tuyen Ho, Souradip Chakraborty, Xiyao Wang, Furong Huang
First: 2026-03-09T17:58:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T17:58:56+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://attention-is-all-i-need.github.io/ACT/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Training large language models (LLMs) as autonomous agents often begins with imitation learning, but it only teaches agents what to do without understanding why: agents never contrast successful actions against suboptimal alternatives and thus lack awareness of action quality. Recent approaches attempt to address this by introducing self-reflection supervision derived from contrasts between expert and alternative actions. However, the training paradigm fundamentally remains imitation learning: the model imitates pre-constructed reflection text rather than learning to reason autonomously. We propose Agentic Critical Training (ACT), a reinforcement learning paradigm that trains agents to identify the better action among alternatives. By rewarding whether the model's judgment is correct, ACT drives the model to autonomously develop reasoning about action quality, producing genuine self-reflection rather than imitating it. Across three challenging agent benchmarks, ACT consistently improves agent performance when combined with different post-training methods. It achieves an average improvement of 5.07 points over imitation learning and 4.62 points over reinforcement learning. Compared to approaches that inject reflection capability through knowledge distillation, ACT also demonstrates clear advantages, yielding an average improvement of 2.42 points. Moreover, ACT enables strong out-of-distribution generalization on agentic benchmarks and improves performance on general reasoning benchmarks without any reasoning-specific training data, highlighting the value of our method. These results suggest that ACT is a promising path toward developing more reflective and capable LLM agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：智能体批判性训练
将大型语言模型（LLM）训练为自主智能体通常从模仿学习开始，但这仅教会智能体执行动作而不理解原因：智能体从未对比成功动作与次优替代方案，因而缺乏对动作质量的认知。近期研究尝试通过引入专家动作与替代动作对比衍生的自反思监督来解决此问题。然而训练范式本质上仍是模仿学习：模型模仿预先构建的反思文本，而非学习自主推理。我们提出智能体批判性训练（ACT），这是一种强化学习范式，训练智能体在替代动作中识别更优选择。通过奖励模型判断的正确性，ACT驱动模型自主形成对动作质量的推理能力，产生真正的自反思而非模仿。在三个具有挑战性的智能体基准测试中，ACT与不同后训练方法结合时均能持续提升智能体性能，相较模仿学习平均提升5.07分，相较强化学习平均提升4.62分。与通过知识蒸馏注入反思能力的方法相比，ACT也展现出明显优势，平均提升2.42分。此外，ACT在智能体基准测试中实现了强大的分布外泛化能力，并在未使用任何推理专项训练数据的情况下，提升了通用推理基准测试的性能，凸显了本方法的价值。这些结果表明ACT是开发更具反思性和能力的大型语言模型智能体的可行路径。

To address this, ACT introduces a reinforcement learning paradigm where agents are trained to identify superior actions among alternatives by rewarding correct judgments, thereby fostering autonomous reasoning about action quality rather than merely imitating pre-constructed reflection text. Experimental results across three challenging agent benchmarks show that ACT consistently enhances performance, achieving average improvements of 5.07 points over imitation learning and 4.62 points over reinforcement learning, while also demonstrating strong out-of-distribution generalization and benefits on general reasoning tasks without specific training data.

DemoDiffusion: One-Shot Human Imitation using pre-trained Diffusion Policy
Authors: Sungjae Park, Homanga Bharadhwaj, Shubham Tulsiani
Venue: ICRA 2026
First: 2025-06-25T17:59:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T17:58:20+00:00
Comments: 11 pages. Published at ICRA 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We propose DemoDiffusion, a simple method for enabling robots to perform manipulation tasks by imitating a single human demonstration, without requiring task-specific training or paired human-robot data. Our approach is based on two insights. First, the hand motion in a human demonstration provides a useful prior for the robot's end-effector trajectory, which we can convert into a rough open-loop robot motion trajectory via kinematic retargeting. Second, while this retargeted motion captures the overall structure of the task, it may not align well with plausible robot actions in-context. To address this, we leverage a pre-trained generalist diffusion policy to modify the trajectory, ensuring it both follows the human motion and remains within the distribution of plausible robot actions. Unlike approaches based on online reinforcement learning or paired human-robot data, our method enables robust adaptation to new tasks and scenes with minimal effort. In real-world experiments across 8 diverse manipulation tasks, DemoDiffusion achieves 83.8\% average success rate, compared to 13.8\% for the pre-trained policy and 52.5\% for kinematic retargeting, succeeding even on tasks where the pre-trained generalist policy fails entirely. Project page: https://demodiffusion.github.io/
中文标题/摘要
标题：DemoDiffusion：基于预训练扩散策略的单次人类模仿方法
我们提出DemoDiffusion，一种使机器人通过单次人类演示即可执行操作任务的简易方法，无需任务特定训练或配对人机数据。该方法基于两点洞见：首先，人类演示中的手部运动为机器人末端执行器轨迹提供了有效先验，可通过运动学重定向转化为粗略的开环机器人运动轨迹；其次，重定向轨迹虽能捕捉任务整体结构，但可能与实际场景中的合理机器人动作存在偏差。为此，我们利用预训练的通用扩散策略修正轨迹，确保其既遵循人类运动模式，又保持在合理机器人动作分布内。与基于在线强化学习或配对人机数据的方法不同，本方法能以最小成本实现对新任务和场景的鲁棒适应。在8项多样化操作任务的真实实验中，DemoDiffusion平均成功率达83.8%，显著优于预训练策略的13.8%和运动学重定向的52.5%，甚至在预训练通用策略完全失败的任务中仍能成功。项目页面：https://demodiffusion.github.io/
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for robots to learn manipulation tasks from minimal human input without task-specific training, this paper introduces DemoDiffusion, a method for one-shot human imitation. The approach first extracts a rough robot motion trajectory from a single human demonstration via kinematic retargeting of hand motion, then refines it using a pre-trained generalist diffusion policy to ensure the trajectory aligns with plausible robot actions while following the human intent. Experimental results across eight diverse real-world manipulation tasks show an average success rate of 83.8%, significantly outperforming both the pre-trained policy alone (13.8%) and basic kinematic retargeting (52.5%), and demonstrating robust adaptation to new tasks where the generalist policy fails.

Tree-based Dialogue Reinforced Policy Optimization for Red-Teaming Attacks
Authors: Ruohao Guo, Afshin Oroojlooy, Roshan Sridhar, Miguel Ballesteros, Alan Ritter, Dan Roth
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-02T17:57:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T17:54:56+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite recent rapid progress in AI safety, current large language models remain vulnerable to adversarial attacks in multi-turn interaction settings, where attackers strategically adapt their prompts across conversation turns and pose a more critical yet realistic challenge. Existing approaches that discover safety vulnerabilities either rely on manual red-teaming with human experts or employ automated methods using pre-defined templates and human-curated attack data, with most focusing on single-turn attacks. However, these methods did not explore the vast space of possible multi-turn attacks, failing to consider novel attack trajectories that emerge from complex dialogue dynamics and strategic conversation planning. This gap is particularly critical given recent findings that LLMs exhibit significantly higher vulnerability to multi-turn attacks compared to single-turn attacks. We propose DialTree, an on-policy reinforcement learning framework integrated with tree search that autonomously discovers diverse multi-turn attack strategies by treating the dialogue as a sequential decision-making problem, enabling systematic exploration without manually curated data. Through extensive experiments, our approach not only achieves more than 44.2% higher ASR across 12 target models compared to previous state-of-the-art approaches, but also effectively uncovers new attack strategies by learning optimal dialogue policies that maximize attack success across multiple turns.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于树形对话的强化策略优化在红队攻击中的应用
尽管人工智能安全领域近期进展迅速，当前大语言模型在多轮交互场景中仍易受对抗性攻击。攻击者通过跨对话轮次策略性调整提示，构成更严峻且现实的挑战。现有发现安全漏洞的方法依赖人工专家红队测试，或采用基于预定义模板和人工标注攻击数据的自动化方法，且多聚焦单轮攻击。然而，这些方法未探索多轮攻击的广阔可能性空间，未能考虑复杂对话动态和策略性会话规划产生的新型攻击轨迹。鉴于近期研究发现大语言模型对多轮攻击的脆弱性显著高于单轮攻击，这一空白尤为关键。我们提出DialTree框架：一种集成树搜索的在线策略强化学习方法，通过将对话建模为序列决策问题，无需人工标注数据即可系统化探索并自主发现多样化的多轮攻击策略。大量实验表明，该方法在12个目标模型上的攻击成功率较先前最优方法提升超44.2%，并能通过学习最大化多轮攻击成功概率的最优对话策略，有效揭示新型攻击模式。

How Far Can Unsupervised RLVR Scale LLM Training?
Authors: Bingxiang He, Yuxin Zuo, Zeyuan Liu, Shangziqi Zhao, Zixuan Fu, Junlin Yang, Cheng Qian, Kaiyan Zhang, Yuchen Fan, Ganqu Cui, Xiusi Chen, Youbang Sun, Xingtai Lv, Xuekai Zhu, Li Sheng, Ran Li, Huan-ang Gao, Yuchen Zhang, Bowen Zhou, Zhiyuan Liu, Ning Ding
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-09T17:38:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T17:38:11+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unsupervised reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (URLVR) offers a pathway to scale LLM training beyond the supervision bottleneck by deriving rewards without ground truth labels. Recent works leverage model intrinsic signals, showing promising early gains, yet their potential and limitations remain unclear. In this work, we revisit URLVR and provide a comprehensive analysis spanning taxonomy, theory and extensive experiments. We first classify URLVR methods into intrinsic versus external based on reward sources, then establish a unified theoretical framework revealing that all intrinsic methods converge toward sharpening the model's initial distribution This sharpening mechanism succeeds when initial confidence aligns with correctness but fails catastrophically when misaligned. Through systematic experiments, we show intrinsic rewards consistently follow a rise-then-fall pattern across methods, with collapse timing determined by model prior rather than engineering choices. Despite these scaling limits, we find intrinsic rewards remain valuable in test-time training on small datasets, and propose Model Collapse Step to measure model prior, serving as a practical indicator for RL trainability. Finally, we explore external reward methods that ground verification in computational asymmetries, showing preliminary evidence they may escape the confidence-correctness ceiling. Our findings chart boundaries for intrinsic URLVR while motivating paths toward scalable alternatives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无监督RLVR能将LLM训练扩展到何种程度？
基于可验证奖励的无监督强化学习（URLVR）通过无需真实标签生成奖励，为突破监督瓶颈扩展大语言模型训练提供了路径。近期研究利用模型内在信号展现出早期潜力，但其潜力与局限尚不明确。本文重新审视URLVR，从分类体系、理论框架及大量实验进行全面分析。首先依据奖励来源将URLVR方法分为内在型与外部型，继而建立统一理论框架，揭示所有内在方法均趋于强化模型的初始分布——当初始置信度与正确性一致时该机制有效，但二者错位时将导致灾难性失效。系统实验表明，内在奖励在所有方法中均呈现先升后降的模式，其崩溃时机由模型先验而非工程选择决定。尽管存在扩展限制，我们发现内在奖励在小数据集测试时训练中仍有价值，并提出“模型崩溃步数”作为衡量模型先验的指标，为RL可训练性提供实践参照。最后，我们探索了基于计算不对称性进行验证的外部奖励方法，初步证据显示其可能突破置信度-正确性天花板。本研究界定了内在URLVR的边界，并为探索可扩展替代方案指明方向。

This paper investigates the scalability of unsupervised reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (URLVR) for large language model training, motivated by the need to overcome supervision bottlenecks. The authors classify URLVR methods into intrinsic and external reward types, establishing a theoretical framework that reveals intrinsic methods converge toward sharpening the model's initial distribution, which succeeds only when initial confidence aligns with correctness. Experimental results demonstrate that intrinsic rewards consistently exhibit a rise-then-fall pattern, with collapse timing dictated by model prior rather than engineering, yet remain useful for test-time training on small datasets; external reward methods show preliminary potential to surpass these limitations by leveraging computational asymmetries.
本文研究了无监督可验证奖励强化学习在大型语言模型训练中的可扩展性，旨在突破监督学习的瓶颈。作者将URLVR方法分为内在奖励和外部奖励两类，并建立了一个理论框架，揭示内在奖励方法会收敛于强化模型的初始分布，仅当初始置信度与正确性一致时有效。实验结果表明，内在奖励普遍呈现先升后降的模式，其崩溃时间由模型先验决定而非工程选择，但在小数据集上的测试时训练中仍有价值；外部奖励方法通过利用计算不对称性，初步显示出可能超越这些限制的潜力。
Towards Batch-to-Streaming Deep Reinforcement Learning for Continuous Control
Authors: Riccardo De Monte, Matteo Cederle, Gian Antonio Susto
First: 2026-03-09T16:40:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T16:40:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
State-of-the-art deep reinforcement learning (RL) methods have achieved remarkable performance in continuous control tasks, yet their computational complexity is often incompatible with the constraints of resource-limited hardware, due to their reliance on replay buffers, batch updates, and target networks. The emerging paradigm of streaming deep RL addresses this limitation through purely online updates, achieving strong empirical performance on standard benchmarks. In this work, we propose two novel streaming deep RL algorithms, Streaming Soft Actor-Critic (S2AC) and Streaming Deterministic Actor-Critic (SDAC), explicitly designed to be compatible with state-of-the-art batch RL methods, making them particularly suitable for on-device finetuning applications such as Sim2Real transfer. Both algorithms achieve performance comparable to state-of-the-art streaming baselines on standard benchmarks without requiring tedious hyperparameter tuning. Finally, we further investigate the practical challenges of transitioning from batch to streaming learning during finetuning and propose concrete strategies to tackle them.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向连续控制的批处理到流式深度强化学习研究
当前最先进的深度强化学习方法在连续控制任务中取得了显著性能，但由于其依赖经验回放缓冲区、批量更新和目标网络，计算复杂度常与资源受限硬件的约束不兼容。新兴的流式深度强化学习范式通过纯在线更新解决了这一局限，在标准基准测试中实现了强大的实证性能。本研究提出了两种新型流式深度强化学习算法——流式软演员-评论家（S2AC）与流式确定性演员-评论家（SDAC），其设计明确兼容最先进的批处理方法，尤其适用于仿真到现实迁移等设备端微调应用。两种算法在标准基准测试中均达到与前沿流式基线相当的性能，且无需繁琐的超参数调优。最后，我们进一步探究了微调过程中从批处理转向流式学习的实际挑战，并提出了具体应对策略。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to adapt high-performing but computationally heavy batch deep reinforcement learning (RL) methods for continuous control to resource-constrained hardware, which is crucial for applications like on-device Sim2Real transfer. To address this, the authors propose two novel streaming deep RL algorithms, Streaming Soft Actor-Critic (S2AC) and Streaming Deterministic Actor-Critic (SDAC), designed to be compatible with state-of-the-art batch methods and operate with purely online updates. The main experimental results demonstrate that both algorithms achieve performance comparable to existing streaming baselines on standard benchmarks without extensive hyperparameter tuning, and the work further investigates and proposes strategies to overcome practical challenges in transitioning from batch to streaming learning during finetuning.
本文的研究动机源于需要将高性能但计算量大的批量深度强化学习方法适配到资源受限的硬件上，这对于设备端的仿真到现实迁移等应用至关重要。为此，作者提出了两种新颖的流式深度强化学习算法：流式软演员-评论家（S2AC）和流式确定性演员-评论家（SDAC），这些算法设计为与先进的批量方法兼容，并采用纯在线更新。主要实验结果表明，两种算法在标准基准测试上取得了与现有流式基线相当的性能，且无需繁琐的超参数调整；研究还进一步探讨了在微调过程中从批量学习过渡到流式学习的实际挑战，并提出了具体的解决策略。
MetaWorld-X: Hierarchical World Modeling via VLM-Orchestrated Experts for Humanoid Loco-Manipulation
Authors: Yutong Shen, Hangxu Liu, Penghui Liu, Jiashuo Luo, Yongkang Zhang, Rex Morvley, Chen Jiang, Jianwei Zhang, Lei Zhang
First: 2026-03-09T16:28:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T16:28:26+00:00
Comments: 8 figures, https://syt2004.github.io/metaworldX/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Learning natural, stable, and compositionally generalizable whole-body control policies for humanoid robots performing simultaneous locomotion and manipulation (loco-manipulation) remains a fundamental challenge in robotics. Existing reinforcement learning approaches typically rely on a single monolithic policy to acquire multiple skills, which often leads to cross-skill gradient interference and motion pattern conflicts in high-degree-of-freedom systems. As a result, generated behaviors frequently exhibit unnatural movements, limited stability, and poor generalization to complex task compositions. To address these limitations, we propose MetaWorld-X, a hierarchical world model framework for humanoid control. Guided by a divide-and-conquer principle, our method decomposes complex control problems into a set of specialized expert policies (Specialized Expert Policies, SEP). Each expert is trained under human motion priors through imitation-constrained reinforcement learning, introducing biomechanically consistent inductive biases that ensure natural and physically plausible motion generation. Building upon this foundation, we further develop an Intelligent Routing Mechanism (IRM) supervised by a Vision-Language Model (VLM), enabling semantic-driven expert composition. The VLM-guided router dynamically integrates expert policies according to high-level task semantics, facilitating compositional generalization and adaptive execution in multi-stage loco-manipulation tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MetaWorld-X：基于VLM编排专家策略的人形机器人分层世界建模与移动操作控制
为人形机器人实现自然、稳定且具备组合泛化能力的全身控制策略（同时进行移动与操作）是机器人学的核心挑战。现有强化学习方法通常依赖单一整体策略学习多种技能，在高自由度系统中易导致技能间梯度干扰与运动模式冲突，致使生成动作常出现非自然运动、稳定性不足及对复杂任务组合泛化能力差等问题。为此，我们提出MetaWorld-X——一种面向人形机器人控制的分层世界模型框架。基于分治原则，该方法将复杂控制问题分解为一组专用专家策略，各专家通过模仿约束强化学习在人体运动先验指导下训练，引入生物力学一致的归纳偏置以确保生成自然且物理合理的运动。在此基础上，我们进一步开发了由视觉语言模型监督的智能路由机制，实现语义驱动的专家策略组合。VLM引导的路由器依据高层任务语义动态整合专家策略，促进多阶段移动操作任务中的组合泛化与自适应执行。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of monolithic reinforcement learning policies for humanoid loco-manipulation, which often produce unnatural, unstable motions with poor compositional generalization. The method, MetaWorld-X, employs a hierarchical world model that decomposes control into specialized expert policies trained with human motion priors via imitation-constrained RL, ensuring biomechanically plausible movements, and integrates them via a Vision-Language Model-guided intelligent routing mechanism for semantic-driven composition. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach generates more natural, stable behaviors and achieves superior compositional generalization in complex multi-stage loco-manipulation tasks compared to prior methods.
本研究的动机是解决人形机器人全身运动操控中单一强化学习策略常导致动作不自然、不稳定且组合泛化能力差的问题。该方法提出MetaWorld-X分层世界模型框架，将复杂控制分解为多个通过模仿约束强化学习结合人类运动先验训练的专业策略，确保生物力学合理的运动生成，并利用视觉语言模型监督的智能路由机制进行语义驱动的策略组合。实验结果表明，该方法能产生更自然稳定的行为，并在复杂多阶段运动操控任务中实现了优于现有方法的组合泛化性能。
RetroAgent: From Solving to Evolving via Retrospective Dual Intrinsic Feedback
Authors: Xiaoying Zhang, Zichen Liu, Yipeng Zhang, Xia Hu, Wenqi Shao
First: 2026-03-09T16:23:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T16:23:33+00:00
Comments: 45 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM)-based agents trained with reinforcement learning (RL) have shown strong potential on complex interactive tasks. However, standard RL paradigms favor static problem-solving over continuous adaptation: agents often converge to suboptimal strategies due to insufficient exploration, while learned knowledge remains implicit within parameters rather than explicitly retrievable, limiting effective experiential learning. To address these limitations, we introduce RetroAgent, an online RL framework that empowers agents to master complex interactive environments not just by solving, but by evolving. Concretely, RetroAgent features a hindsight self-reflection mechanism that produces dual intrinsic feedback: (1) intrinsic numerical feedback that that tracks incremental subtask completion relative to prior attempts, rewarding promising explorations, and (2) intrinsic language feedback that distills reusable lessons into a memory buffer, retrieved via our proposed Similarity & Utility-Aware Upper Confidence Bound (SimUtil-UCB) strategy balancing relevance, utility, and exploration to effectively leverage past experiences. Extensive experiments on two model families across four challenging agentic tasks demonstrate that RetroAgent significantly outperforms existing methods, achieving state-of-the-art results -- e.g., surpassing Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO)-trained agents by +18.3% on ALFWorld, +15.4% on WebShop, +27.1% on Sokoban, and +8.9% on MineSweeper -- while exhibiting strong test-time adaptation and generalization to out-of-distribution scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RetroAgent：通过回顾式双重内在反馈实现从求解到进化的跨越
基于大语言模型（LLM）并通过强化学习（RL）训练的智能体在复杂交互任务中展现出巨大潜力。然而，标准RL范式偏向静态问题求解而非持续适应：智能体常因探索不足而收敛至次优策略，且习得知识仅隐式存储于参数中而非显式可检索，限制了有效的经验学习。为突破这些局限，我们提出RetroAgent——一种在线RL框架，使智能体不仅能通过求解，更能通过进化来掌握复杂交互环境。具体而言，RetroAgent具备事后自省机制，可生成双重内在反馈：（1）追踪相较于先前尝试的子任务完成进度的内在数值反馈，以奖励有潜力的探索；（2）将可复用经验提炼至记忆缓冲区的内在语言反馈，通过我们提出的相似性与效用感知上置信界（SimUtil-UCB）策略进行检索，该策略平衡相关性、效用性与探索性，从而有效利用过往经验。在两类模型族、四项挑战性智能体任务上的大量实验表明，RetroAgent显著优于现有方法，取得最先进成果——例如在ALFWorld超越GRPO训练智能体18.3%、WebShop提升15.4%、Sokoban提高27.1%、MineSweeper增长8.9%——同时展现出强大的测试时适应能力及对分布外场景的泛化性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of standard reinforcement learning paradigms for LLM-based agents, which often lead to suboptimal strategies and implicit knowledge that hinders continuous adaptation, this paper introduces RetroAgent, an online RL framework featuring a hindsight self-reflection mechanism that generates dual intrinsic feedback. The method combines intrinsic numerical feedback to reward incremental subtask progress and intrinsic language feedback that distills reusable lessons into a memory buffer, retrieved via a novel Similarity & Utility-Aware Upper Confidence Bound strategy to balance relevance, utility, and exploration. Experimental results across four challenging tasks show that RetroAgent significantly outperforms existing methods, achieving state-of-the-art performance with improvements of up to +27.1% and demonstrating strong test-time adaptation and generalization.
本文的动机是标准强化学习范式在基于大语言模型的智能体上存在局限，常导致策略次优且知识隐式化，阻碍持续适应，为此提出了RetroAgent这一在线强化学习框架，其核心是事后自我反思机制，可产生双重内在反馈。该方法结合了用于奖励增量子任务进展的内在数值反馈，以及将可重用经验提炼到记忆缓冲区的内在语言反馈，并通过新颖的相似性与效用感知上置信界策略进行检索，以平衡相关性、效用和探索。在四个挑战性任务上的实验结果表明，RetroAgent显著优于现有方法，实现了最先进的性能，提升幅度最高达+27.1%，并展现出强大的测试时适应和泛化能力。
Impact of Connectivity on Laplacian Representations in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tommaso Giorgi, Pierriccardo Olivieri, Keyue Jiang, Laura Toni, Matteo Papini
First: 2026-03-09T16:20:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T16:20:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning compact state representations in Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) has proven crucial for addressing the curse of dimensionality in large-scale reinforcement learning (RL) problems. Existing principled approaches leverage structural priors on the MDP by constructing state representations as linear combinations of the state-graph Laplacian eigenvectors. When the transition graph is unknown or the state space is prohibitively large, the graph spectral features can be estimated directly via sample trajectories. In this work, we prove an upper bound on the approximation error of linear value function approximation under the learned spectral features. We show how this error scales with the algebraic connectivity of the state-graph, grounding the approximation quality in the topological structure of the MDP. We further bound the error introduced by the eigenvector estimation itself, leading to an end-to-end error decomposition across the representation learning pipeline. Additionally, our expression of the Laplacian operator for the RL setting, although equivalent to existing ones, prevents some common misunderstandings, of which we show some examples from the literature. Our results hold for general (non-uniform) policies without any assumptions on the symmetry of the induced transition kernel. We validate our theoretical findings with numerical simulations on gridworld environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连通性对强化学习中拉普拉斯表示的影响
在马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中学习紧凑的状态表示，已被证明对解决大规模强化学习（RL）问题中的维度灾难至关重要。现有原理性方法通过将状态表示构建为状态图拉普拉斯特征向量的线性组合，来利用MDP的结构先验。当转移图未知或状态空间过大时，可通过采样轨迹直接估计图谱特征。本文证明了在习得谱特征下线性值函数逼近的近似误差上界，并展示了该误差如何随状态图的代数连通性变化，从而将逼近质量锚定于MDP的拓扑结构中。我们进一步界定了特征向量估计本身引入的误差，实现了对表示学习流程的端到端误差分解。此外，我们提出的RL场景下拉普拉斯算子表达式（虽与现有形式等价）避免了文献中常见的误解，并列举了相关示例。我们的结论适用于一般（非均匀）策略，且无需对诱导转移核的对称性作任何假设。最后，通过网格世界环境的数值模拟验证了理论结果。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the impact of state-graph connectivity on the quality of Laplacian-based state representations in reinforcement learning, motivated by the need for compact representations to combat dimensionality in large MDPs. The method involves deriving an upper bound on the approximation error for linear value functions when using estimated spectral features from sample trajectories, explicitly linking this error to the algebraic connectivity of the underlying graph and bounding the error from eigenvector estimation. Experimental validation through gridworld simulations confirms the theoretical results, showing how approximation quality depends on the MDP's topological structure without requiring assumptions on policy uniformity or transition kernel symmetry.
本文研究了状态图连通性对强化学习中基于拉普拉斯算子的状态表示质量的影响，其动机是为解决大规模马尔可夫决策过程中的维度灾难问题需要紧凑的表示。该方法通过从样本轨迹估计谱特征，推导了线性值函数近似误差的上界，明确将此误差与底层图的代数连通性联系起来，并限制了特征向量估计本身引入的误差。在网格世界环境中的数值模拟验证了理论结果，表明近似质量如何依赖于马尔可夫决策过程的拓扑结构，且无需对策略均匀性或转移核对称性进行假设。
Breaking the Bias Barrier in Concave Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Swetha Ganesh, Vaneet Aggarwal
First: 2026-03-09T15:49:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T15:49:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While standard reinforcement learning optimizes a single reward signal, many applications require optimizing a nonlinear utility $f(J_1^π,\dots,J_M^π)$ over multiple objectives, where each $J_m^π$ denotes the expected discounted return of a distinct reward function. A common approach is concave scalarization, which captures important trade-offs such as fairness and risk sensitivity. However, nonlinear scalarization introduces a fundamental challenge for policy gradient methods: the gradient depends on $\partial f(J^π)$, while in practice only empirical return estimates $\hat J$ are available. Because $f$ is nonlinear, the plug-in estimator is biased ($\mathbb{E}[\partial f(\hat J)] \neq \partial f(\mathbb{E}[\hat J])$), leading to persistent gradient bias that degrades sample complexity. In this work we identify and overcome this bias barrier in concave-scalarized multi-objective reinforcement learning. We show that existing policy-gradient methods suffer an intrinsic $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-4})$ sample complexity due to this bias. To address this issue, we develop a Natural Policy Gradient (NPG) algorithm equipped with a multi-level Monte Carlo (MLMC) estimator that controls the bias of the scalarization gradient while maintaining low sampling cost. We prove that this approach achieves the optimal $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ sample complexity for computing an $ε$-optimal policy. Furthermore, we show that when the scalarization function is second-order smooth, the first-order bias cancels automatically, allowing vanilla NPG to achieve the same $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ rate without MLMC. Our results provide the first optimal sample complexity guarantees for concave multi-objective reinforcement learning under policy-gradient methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破凹性多目标强化学习中的偏差壁垒
标准强化学习仅优化单一奖励信号，而许多应用需要在多个目标上优化非线性效用函数 $f(J_1^π,\dots,J_M^π)$，其中每个 $J_m^π$ 表示不同奖励函数的期望折扣回报。常用方法是凹标量化，它能捕捉公平性、风险敏感性等重要权衡。然而，非线性标量化给策略梯度方法带来根本性挑战：梯度依赖于 $\partial f(J^π)$，而实践中仅能获得经验回报估计 $\hat J$。由于 $f$ 的非线性特性，插件估计量存在偏差（$\mathbb{E}[\partial f(\hat J)] \neq \partial f(\mathbb{E}[\hat J])$），导致持续梯度偏差并恶化样本复杂度。 本研究识别并克服了凹标量化多目标强化学习中的这一偏差壁垒。我们证明现有策略梯度方法因该偏差存在固有的 $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-4})$ 样本复杂度。为解决此问题，我们开发了配备多级蒙特卡洛估计器的自然策略梯度算法，该算法在控制标量化梯度偏差的同时保持较低采样成本。我们证明该方法在计算 $ε$ 最优策略时达到了最优的 $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ 样本复杂度。此外，当标量化函数满足二阶光滑性时，一阶偏差会自动抵消，使得基础自然策略梯度算法无需多级蒙特卡洛即可实现相同的 $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ 收敛速率。我们的研究首次为策略梯度方法下的凹性多目标强化学习提供了最优样本复杂度保证。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the bias problem in multi-objective reinforcement learning when using concave scalarization to optimize a nonlinear utility over multiple reward signals, a common need for applications like fairness and risk sensitivity. The authors identify that standard policy gradient methods suffer from persistent gradient bias due to the nonlinearity, leading to suboptimal sample complexity of O(ε⁻⁴). To overcome this, they propose a Natural Policy Gradient algorithm with a multi-level Monte Carlo estimator that controls bias efficiently, achieving an optimal sample complexity of O(ε⁻²) for finding an ε-optimal policy. Additionally, they show that for second-order smooth scalarization functions, vanilla NPG can automatically cancel first-order bias and attain the same optimal rate without the need for the advanced estimator.
本文针对多目标强化学习中，使用凹标量化优化多个奖励信号的非线性效用时存在的偏差问题，这在公平性和风险敏感等应用中很常见。作者指出，由于非线性特性，标准策略梯度方法会遭受持续的梯度偏差，导致样本复杂度高达O(ε⁻⁴)。为解决此问题，他们提出了一种结合多级蒙特卡洛估计器的自然策略梯度算法，能有效控制偏差，实现了寻找ε最优策略的最优样本复杂度O(ε⁻²)。此外，他们还证明，对于二阶光滑的标量化函数，普通自然策略梯度可以自动消除一阶偏差，无需高级估计器即可达到相同的最优速率。
Oracle-Guided Soft Shielding for Safe Move Prediction in Chess
Authors: Prajit T Rajendran, Fabio Arnez, Huascar Espinoza, Agnes Delaborde, Chokri Mraidha
First: 2026-03-09T15:40:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T15:40:01+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication at the 24th International Conference on Machine Learning and Applications (ICMLA), 2025. Preprint version in Arxiv
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In high stakes environments, agents relying purely on imitation learning or reinforcement learning often struggle to avoid safety-critical errors during exploration. Existing reinforcement learning approaches for environments such as chess require hundreds of thousands of episodes and substantial computational resources to converge. Imitation learning, on the other hand, is more sample efficient but is brittle under distributional shift and lacks mechanisms for proactive risk avoidance. In this work, we propose Oracle-Guided Soft Shielding (OGSS), a simple yet effective framework for safer decision-making, enabling safe exploration by learning a probabilistic safety model from oracle feedback in an imitation learning setting. Focusing on the domain of chess, we train a model to predict strong moves based on past games, and separately learn a blunder prediction model from Stockfish evaluations to estimate the tactical risk of each move. During inference, the agent first generates a set of candidate moves and then uses the blunder model to determine high-risk options, and uses a utility function combining the predicted move likelihood from the policy model and the blunder probability to select actions that strike a balance between performance and safety. This enables the agent to explore and play competitively while significantly reducing the chance of tactical mistakes. Across hundreds of games against a strong chess engine, we compare our approach with other methods in the literature, such as action pruning, SafeDAgger, and uncertainty-based sampling. Our results demonstrate that OGSS variants maintain a lower blunder rate even as the agent's exploration ratio is increased by several folds, highlighting its ability to support broader exploration without compromising tactical soundness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：国际象棋安全走子预测的Oracle引导软屏蔽方法
在高风险环境中，仅依赖模仿学习或强化学习的智能体在探索过程中常难以避免安全关键错误。现有针对国际象棋等环境的强化学习方法需要数十万次对局和大量计算资源才能收敛；模仿学习虽样本效率更高，但在分布偏移下表现脆弱且缺乏主动风险规避机制。本研究提出Oracle引导软屏蔽（OGSS）框架，通过从模仿学习环境中的oracle反馈学习概率安全模型，实现更安全的决策与探索。在国际象棋领域，我们训练模型基于历史对局预测强着，并另从Stockfish评估数据训练失误预测模型以估计每步棋的战术风险。推理时，智能体首先生成候选着法集合，随后利用失误模型识别高风险选项，并通过结合策略模型的着法预测概率与失误概率的效用函数，选择兼顾性能与安全的行动。该方法使智能体能在保持竞技水平的同时显著降低战术失误概率。在与强象棋引擎的数百局对弈中，我们将OGSS与动作剪枝、SafeDAgger及基于不确定性的采样等方法对比。结果表明，即使智能体探索率提升数倍，OGSS变体仍能保持更低的失误率，突显其在支持广泛探索时不损害战术稳健性的能力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for safer decision-making in high-stakes environments where pure imitation or reinforcement learning often leads to safety-critical errors or inefficiency, this paper proposes Oracle-Guided Soft Shielding (OGSS), a framework that combines a policy model for predicting strong moves with a separately learned blunder prediction model from oracle feedback to estimate tactical risk. The method operates by generating candidate moves and then using a utility function to balance the policy's move likelihood against the blunder probability, thereby selecting actions that maintain performance while reducing risk. Experimental results in chess, tested across hundreds of games against a strong engine, show that OGSS variants achieve a lower blunder rate compared to methods like action pruning and SafeDAgger, even when exploration is increased severalfold, demonstrating robust safety without compromising tactical soundness.
本文的动机是解决高风险环境中纯模仿学习或强化学习易导致安全关键错误或效率低下的问题，为此提出了Oracle-Guided Soft Shielding（OGSS）框架，该方法结合了用于预测强着法的策略模型和从先知反馈中单独学习的失误预测模型来评估战术风险。其方法首先生成候选着法，然后通过一个效用函数平衡策略的着法似然与失误概率，从而选择在保持性能的同时降低风险的行动。在国际象棋领域的实验结果表明，在与强大引擎进行的数百局对弈中，OGSS变体相比动作剪枝、SafeDAgger等方法，即使在探索率提高数倍的情况下仍能保持较低的失误率，证明了其在保障战术稳健性的同时实现了更强的安全性。
Integrating Lagrangian Neural Networks into the Dyna Framework for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shreya Das, Kundan Kumar, Muhammad Iqbal, Outi Savolainen, Dominik Baumann, Laura Ruotsalainen, Simo Särkkä
First: 2026-03-09T15:06:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T15:06:10+00:00
Comments: 5 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) is sample-efficient but depends on the accuracy of the learned dynamics, which are often modeled using black-box methods that do not adhere to physical laws. Those methods tend to produce inaccurate predictions when presented with data that differ from the original training set. In this work, we employ Lagrangian neural networks (LNNs), which enforce an underlying Lagrangian structure to train the model within a Dyna-based MBRL framework. Furthermore, we train the LNN using stochastic gradient-based and state-estimation-based optimizers to learn the network's weights. The state-estimation-based method converges faster than the stochastic gradient-based method during neural network training. Simulation results are provided to illustrate the effectiveness of the proposed LNN-based Dyna framework for MBRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：将拉格朗日神经网络集成至强化学习的Dyna框架中
基于模型的强化学习（MBRL）具有样本效率高的优势，但其性能依赖于学习到的动力学模型的准确性。现有方法多采用黑箱模型，这些模型不遵循物理定律，当遇到与原始训练集不同的数据时往往产生不准确的预测。本研究采用拉格朗日神经网络（LNNs），通过强制拉格朗日结构在基于Dyna的MBRL框架内训练模型。此外，我们使用基于随机梯度和基于状态估计的优化器来训练LNN以学习网络权重。在神经网络训练过程中，基于状态估计的方法比基于随机梯度的方法收敛更快。仿真结果验证了所提出的基于LNN的Dyna框架在MBRL中的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This work is motivated by the need to improve the accuracy and physical consistency of learned dynamics models in model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL), as standard black-box models often fail on out-of-distribution data. The method integrates Lagrangian neural networks (LNNs), which embed physical Lagrangian structure, into the Dyna MBRL framework, and employs both stochastic gradient and state-estimation optimizers to train the LNN weights. The main experimental results show that the state-estimation optimizer converges faster during training, and simulations demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed LNN-based Dyna framework for MBRL.
本研究的动机在于提高基于模型的强化学习中动力学模型的准确性和物理一致性，因为标准的黑盒模型在处理分布外数据时常常失效。方法将拉格朗日神经网络集成到Dyna框架中，该网络强制遵循拉格朗日物理结构，并采用随机梯度和状态估计两种优化器来训练网络权重。主要实验结果表明，状态估计优化器在训练中收敛更快，仿真验证了所提出的基于拉格朗日神经网络的Dyna框架在基于模型的强化学习中的有效性。
Reasoning as Compression: Unifying Budget Forcing via the Conditional Information Bottleneck
Authors: Fabio Valerio Massoli, Andrey Kuzmin, Arash Behboodi
First: 2026-03-09T14:56:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:56:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting improves LLM accuracy on complex tasks but often increases token usage and inference cost. Existing "Budget Forcing" methods reducing cost via fine-tuning with heuristic length penalties, suppress both essential reasoning and redundant filler. We recast efficient reasoning as a lossy compression problem under the Information Bottleneck (IB) principle, and identify a key theoretical gap when applying naive IB to transformers: attention violates the Markov property between prompt, reasoning trace, and response. To resolve this issue, we model CoT generation under the Conditional Information Bottleneck (CIB) principle, where the reasoning trace Z acts as a computational bridge that contains only the information about the response Y that is not directly accessible from the prompt X. This yields a general Reinforcement Learning objective: maximize task reward while compressing completions under a prior over reasoning traces, subsuming common heuristics (e.g., length penalties) as special cases (e.g., uniform priors). In contrast to naive token-counting-based approaches, we introduce a semantic prior that measures token cost by surprisal under a language model prior. Empirically, our CIB objective prunes cognitive bloat while preserving fluency and logic, improving accuracy at moderate compression and enabling aggressive compression with minimal accuracy drop.
中文标题/摘要
标题：推理即压缩：通过条件信息瓶颈统一预算约束
思维链提示虽能提升大语言模型在复杂任务上的准确性，但常增加令牌使用量和推理成本。现有“预算约束”方法通过启发式长度惩罚进行微调以降低成本，却同时抑制了关键推理与冗余填充。我们将高效推理重构为信息瓶颈原则下的有损压缩问题，并指出将朴素信息瓶颈应用于Transformer时的关键理论缺陷：注意力机制破坏了提示、推理轨迹与响应之间的马尔可夫性。为解决此问题，我们在条件信息瓶颈原则下建模思维链生成，其中推理轨迹Z作为计算桥梁，仅包含无法直接从提示X获取的响应Y相关信息。由此推导出通用的强化学习目标：在推理轨迹先验下压缩生成内容的同时最大化任务奖励，将常见启发式方法（如长度惩罚）纳入为特例（如均匀先验）。区别于基于令牌计数的朴素方法，我们引入语义先验，通过语言模型先验下的惊异值度量令牌成本。实验表明，我们的条件信息瓶颈目标能在保持流畅性与逻辑性的同时消除认知膨胀，在适度压缩时提升准确性，并在激进压缩时实现最小精度损失。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the trade-off between reasoning accuracy and computational cost in Chain-of-Thought prompting for large language models, where existing budget-forcing methods often indiscriminately compress reasoning traces. To unify and improve upon these heuristics, the authors frame efficient reasoning as a lossy compression problem under the Conditional Information Bottleneck principle, which properly accounts for the non-Markovian nature of transformer attention by treating the reasoning trace as a bridge containing only response-relevant information not directly inferable from the prompt. This yields a reinforcement learning objective that maximizes task reward while compressing completions relative to a prior over traces, subsuming common penalties like length constraints as special cases. Experimental results show that their method, especially when using a semantic prior based on language model surprisal, effectively prunes redundant content while maintaining logical fluency, improving accuracy at moderate compression levels and enabling aggressive compression with minimal accuracy loss.
本文针对大语言模型中思维链提示在提升复杂任务准确性的同时增加计算成本的问题，提出将高效推理重新定义为基于条件信息瓶颈原则的有损压缩任务，以解决现有预算强制方法因启发式长度惩罚而同时抑制关键推理与冗余内容的问题。该方法通过条件信息瓶颈原理建模思维链生成，将推理轨迹视为仅包含无法直接从提示中获取的响应相关信息的计算桥梁，从而克服了朴素信息瓶颈应用于Transformer时因注意力机制违反马尔可夫性的理论缺陷。由此推导出一个统一的强化学习目标，即在最大化任务奖励的同时，依据推理轨迹的先验分布压缩生成内容，将常见的启发式方法（如长度惩罚）涵盖为特例。实验结果表明，该方法尤其在使用基于语言模型惊异度的语义先验时，能有效剔除认知冗余而保持逻辑流畅性，在适度压缩下提升准确性，并在激进压缩时仅导致最小精度下降。
AltNet: Addressing the Plasticity-Stability Dilemma in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mansi Maheshwari, John C. Raisbeck, Bruno Castro da Silva
First: 2025-11-30T19:02:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:52:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Artificial neural networks have shown remarkable success in supervised learning when trained on a single task using a fixed dataset. However, when neural networks are trained on a reinforcement learning task, their ability to continue learning from new experiences declines over time. This decline in learning ability is known as plasticity loss. To restore plasticity, prior work has explored periodically resetting the parameters of the learning network, a strategy that often improves performance. However, such resets come at the cost of a temporary drop in performance, which can be dangerous in real-world settings. To overcome this instability, we introduce AltNet, a reset-based approach that restores plasticity without performance degradation by leveraging a pair of twin networks. The use of twin networks anchors performance during resets through a mechanism that allows networks to periodically alternate roles: one network learns as it acts in the environment, while the other learns off-policy from the active network's interactions through a replay buffer. At fixed intervals, the active network is reset and the passive network, having learned from prior experience, becomes the new active network. AltNet restores plasticity, improving sample efficiency and achieving higher performance, while avoiding performance drops that pose risks in safety-critical settings. We demonstrate these advantages in several high-dimensional control tasks from the DeepMind Control Suite, where AltNet outperforms various relevant baseline methods, as well as state-of-the-art reset-based techniques.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AltNet：解决强化学习中的可塑性-稳定性困境
人工神经网络在使用固定数据集训练单一监督学习任务时表现出显著成功。然而，当神经网络在强化学习任务中训练时，其从新经验中持续学习的能力会随时间下降，这种现象称为可塑性丧失。为恢复可塑性，先前研究探索了周期性重置学习网络参数的方法，该策略常能提升性能，但重置会导致性能暂时下降，在现实场景中可能带来风险。为克服此不稳定性，本文提出AltNet——一种基于重置的方法，通过利用一对孪生网络恢复可塑性且避免性能退化。孪生网络通过周期性角色轮换机制在重置期间锚定性能：一个网络在环境中行动并学习，另一个网络通过经验回放池从主动网络的交互中进行离线学习。在固定间隔，主动网络被重置，而习得先前经验的被动网络成为新的主动网络。AltNet恢复了可塑性，提升了样本效率并实现了更高性能，同时避免了在安全关键场景中构成风险的性能下降。我们在DeepMind控制套件的多个高维控制任务中验证了这些优势，AltNet在此超越了多种相关基线方法及前沿的重置技术。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for AltNet stems from the plasticity-stability dilemma in reinforcement learning, where neural networks lose their ability to learn from new experiences over time, known as plasticity loss, which prior methods address with parameter resets that cause risky performance drops. The method introduces a twin-network architecture where one network actively interacts with the environment while the other learns off-policy from a replay buffer, periodically alternating roles and resetting the active network to restore plasticity without degradation. Experimental results on high-dimensional control tasks from the DeepMind Control Suite show that AltNet improves sample efficiency and achieves higher performance compared to baseline and state-of-the-art reset-based techniques, while avoiding dangerous performance declines.
AltNet的提出动机源于强化学习中的可塑性-稳定性困境，即神经网络随时间推移会丧失从新经验中学习的能力（称为可塑性丧失），先前方法通过参数重置来解决这一问题，但会导致性能下降的风险。该方法采用双网络架构，其中一个网络主动与环境交互，另一个通过回放缓冲区进行离策略学习，定期交换角色并重置主动网络，从而在不降低性能的情况下恢复可塑性。在DeepMind控制套件的高维控制任务实验中，AltNet相比基线方法和先进的基于重置的技术，提高了样本效率并获得了更优性能，同时避免了危险的性能下降。
Mem-T: Densifying Rewards for Long-Horizon Memory Agents
Authors: Yanwei Yue, Boci Peng, Xuanbo Fan, Jiaxin Guo, Qiankun Li, Yan Zhang
First: 2026-01-30T14:23:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:47:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Memory agents, which depart from predefined memory-processing pipelines by endogenously managing the processing, storage, and retrieval of memories, have garnered increasing attention for their autonomy and adaptability. However, existing training paradigms remain constrained: agents often traverse long-horizon sequences of memory operations before receiving sparse and delayed rewards, which hinders truly end-to-end optimization of memory management policies. To address this limitation, we introduce Mem-T, an autonomous memory agent that interfaces with a lightweight hierarchical memory database to perform dynamic updates and multi-turn retrieval over streaming inputs. To effectively train long-horizon memory management capabilities, we further propose MoT-GRPO, a tree-guided reinforcement learning framework that transforms sparse terminal feedback into dense, step-wise supervision via memory operation tree backpropagation and hindsight credit assignment, thereby enabling the joint optimization of memory construction and retrieval. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Mem-T is (1) high-performing, surpassing frameworks such as A-Mem and Mem0 by up to $14.92\%$, and (2) economical, operating on a favorable accuracy-efficiency Pareto frontier and reducing inference tokens per query by $\sim24.45\%$ relative to GAM without sacrificing performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Mem-T：面向长程记忆智能体的奖励稠密化方法

Meta-RL with Shared Representations Enables Fast Adaptation in Energy Systems
Authors: Théo Zangato, Aomar Osmani, Pegah Alizadeh
First: 2026-03-09T14:15:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:15:51+00:00
Comments: accepted at PAKDD 2026, Hong Kong
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Meta-Reinforcement Learning addresses the critical limitations of conventional Reinforcement Learning in multi-task and non-stationary environments by enabling fast policy adaptation and improved generalization. We introduce a novel Meta-RL framework that integrates a bi-level optimization scheme with a hybrid actor-critic architecture specially designed to enhance sample efficiency and inter-task adaptability. To improve knowledge transfer, we meta-learn a shared state feature extractor jointly optimized across actor and critic networks, providing efficient representation learning and limiting overfitting to individual tasks or dominant profiles. Additionally, we propose a parameter-sharing mechanism between the outer- and inner-loop actor networks, to reduce redundant learning and accelerate adaptation during task revisitation. The approach is validated on a real-world Building Energy Management Systems dataset covering nearly a decade of temporal and structural variability, for which we propose a task preparation method to promote generalization. Experiments demonstrate effective task adaptation and better performance compared to conventional RL and Meta-RL methods.
中文标题/摘要
