Aligning to Illusions: Choice Blindness in Human and AI Feedback
Authors: Wenbin Wu
First: 2026-03-09T14:10:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T14:10:36+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 6 figures, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) assumes annotator preferences reflect stable internal states. We challenge this through three experiments spanning the preference pipeline. In a human choice blindness study, 91% of surreptitiously swapped preferences go undetected, extending choice blindness to third-person evaluative comparison of unfamiliar text. Testing fifteen LLM judges as potential replacements, we find detection relies on shallow text matching rather than genuine self-monitoring: removing prior reasoning from context causes blindness to surge from near-zero to over 50%, while explicit social pressure induces near-universal compliance. In a dose-response experiment across two architectures from 86M to 2B parameters, one-sixth to one-third of labels must be corrupted before the reward signal halves, yet standard pairwise accuracy remains virtually unchanged. A Best-of-N evaluation confirms this translates to downstream policy degradation: at 50% corruption, reward-guided selection produces no improvement over random sampling, while the proxy model reports monotonically increasing scores. Together, these results reveal a preference construction problem: the signal entering RLHF is shaped by elicitation context in ways that neither human metacognition, LLM self-monitoring, nor standard evaluation metrics can detect.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对齐幻觉：人类与AI反馈中的选择盲视
基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）假设标注者的偏好反映稳定的内在状态。我们通过三项贯穿偏好处理流程的实验对此提出挑战。在人类选择盲视研究中，91%被暗中替换的偏好未被察觉，将选择盲视现象扩展至对陌生文本的第三人称评价比较。测试十五个作为潜在替代方案的LLM评判者时，我们发现其检测依赖浅层文本匹配而非真正的自我监控：从上下文中移除先前的推理过程会使盲视率从接近零飙升至50%以上，而明确的社会压力则引发近乎普遍的顺从行为。在涵盖8600万至20亿参数的两种架构的剂量反应实验中，需要污染六分之一至三分之一的标签才能使奖励信号减半，但标准成对准确率几乎保持不变。Best-of-N评估证实这会导致下游策略退化：在50%污染率下，奖励引导的选择相比随机采样毫无改进，而代理模型却报告单调递增的分数。这些结果共同揭示了偏好构建问题：进入RLHF的信号受到诱发情境的塑造，这种影响既无法被人类元认知、LLM自我监控察觉，也无法通过标准评估指标检测。
Summary / 总结
This paper challenges the assumption in Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) that human preferences are stable, demonstrating instead that preference signals are highly malleable and constructed during elicitation. The method involves three experiments: a human study showing 'choice blindness' where 91% of surreptitiously swapped preferences go undetected; tests with LLM judges revealing their detection relies on shallow text matching and is easily disrupted by removing prior reasoning or applying social pressure; and a dose-response experiment showing reward models are surprisingly robust to label corruption, requiring one-sixth to one-third of labels to be corrupted before the signal halves, yet standard evaluation metrics like pairwise accuracy fail to detect this. The main experimental results confirm that neither human metacognition, LLM self-monitoring, nor standard metrics can detect these flaws, leading to downstream policy degradation where, at 50% corruption, reward-guided selection offers no improvement over random sampling while proxy scores misleadingly increase.
本文对强化学习从人类反馈中学习所依赖的人类偏好具有稳定性的假设提出挑战，证明偏好信号实际上高度可塑且是在引导过程中构建的。研究方法包括三项实验：一项人类研究显示'选择盲视'现象，即91%被暗中调换的偏好未被察觉；对大型语言模型评判者的测试表明，其检测依赖浅层文本匹配，且移除先前推理或施加社会压力会轻易破坏这种能力；以及一项剂量反应实验显示奖励模型对标签污染具有出乎意料的鲁棒性，需要污染六分之一到三分之一的标签才能使信号减半，但成对准确率等标准评估指标却无法检测此问题。主要实验结果证实，无论是人类元认知、大型语言模型的自我监控还是标准评估指标，都无法检测这些缺陷，从而导致下游策略性能下降：在50%污染率下，基于奖励的筛选与随机采样相比毫无改进，而代理模型的评分却误导性地持续上升。
A Recipe for Stable Offline Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dongsu Lee, Daehee Lee, Amy Zhang
First: 2026-03-09T13:57:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T13:57:08+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite remarkable achievements in single-agent offline reinforcement learning (RL), multi-agent RL (MARL) has struggled to adopt this paradigm, largely persisting with on-policy training and self-play from scratch. One reason for this gap comes from the instability of non-linear value decomposition, leading prior works to avoid complex mixing networks in favor of linear value decomposition (e.g., VDN) with value regularization used in single-agent setups. In this work, we analyze the source of instability in non-linear value decomposition within the offline MARL setting. Our observations confirm that they induce value-scale amplification and unstable optimization. To alleviate this, we propose a simple technique, scale-invariant value normalization (SVN), that stabilizes actor-critic training without altering the Bellman fixed point. Empirically, we examine the interaction among key components of offline MARL (e.g., value decomposition, value learning, and policy extraction) and derive a practical recipe that unlocks its full potential.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种稳定的离线多智能体强化学习方案
尽管单智能体离线强化学习（RL）已取得显著成就，但多智能体强化学习（MARL）在采用这一范式时仍面临困难，大多仍依赖于从头开始的在线策略训练与自我博弈。这一差距的部分原因在于非线性价值分解的不稳定性，导致先前研究为避免复杂混合网络而采用线性价值分解（如VDN），并沿用单智能体设置中的价值正则化方法。本文分析了离线MARL中非线性价值分解不稳定的根源，观察证实其会引发价值尺度放大与优化不稳定问题。为缓解此问题，我们提出一种简单技术——尺度不变价值归一化（SVN），可在不改变贝尔曼不动点的前提下稳定演员-评论家训练。通过实证研究，我们探讨了离线MARL关键组件（如价值分解、价值学习与策略提取）间的相互作用，并推导出一套充分发挥其潜力的实用方案。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the instability of offline multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) when using non-linear value decomposition, which has limited the adoption of offline RL techniques in multi-agent settings. The authors identify that non-linear mixing networks cause value-scale amplification and unstable optimization, and they propose a scale-invariant value normalization (SVN) method to stabilize actor-critic training without changing the Bellman fixed point. Experimental results show that SVN, combined with an analysis of interactions among value decomposition, value learning, and policy extraction, leads to a practical recipe that significantly improves the performance and stability of offline MARL.
本文针对离线多智能体强化学习中非线性价值分解的不稳定性问题展开研究，该问题阻碍了离线强化学习技术在多智能体场景中的应用。作者发现非线性混合网络会导致价值尺度放大和优化不稳定，并提出了一种尺度不变的价值归一化方法，在不改变贝尔曼不动点的前提下稳定演员-评论家训练。实验结果表明，该方法结合对价值分解、价值学习和策略提取等关键组件相互作用的分析，形成了一套实用方案，显著提升了离线多智能体强化学习的性能和稳定性。
Revealing Behavioral Plasticity in Large Language Models: A Token-Conditional Perspective
Authors: Liyuan Mao, Le Yu, Jing Zhou, Chujie Zheng, Bowen Yu, Chang Gao, Shixuan Liu, An Yang, Weinan Zhang, JunYang Lin
First: 2026-03-09T13:56:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T13:56:53+00:00
Comments: Work done during an internship at the Qwen Team, Alibaba Group
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this work, we reveal that Large Language Models (LLMs) possess intrinsic behavioral plasticity-akin to chameleons adapting their coloration to environmental cues-that can be exposed through token-conditional generation and stabilized via reinforcement learning. Specifically, by conditioning generation on carefully selected token prefixes sampled from responses exhibiting desired behaviors, LLMs seamlessly adapt their behavioral modes at inference time (e.g., switching from step-by-step reasoning to direct answering) without retraining. Based on this insight, we propose Token-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (ToCoRL), a principled framework that leverages RL to internalize this chameleon-like plasticity, transforming transient inference-time adaptations into stable and learnable behavioral patterns. ToCoRL guides exploration with token-conditional generation and keep enhancing exploitation, enabling emergence of appropriate behaviors. Extensive experiments show that ToCoRL enables precise behavioral control without capability degradation. Notably, we show that large reasoning models, while performing strongly on complex mathematics, can be effectively adapted to excel at factual question answering, which was a capability previously hindered by their step-by-step reasoning patterns.
中文标题/摘要
标题：揭示大语言模型的行为可塑性：基于令牌条件化的视角
本研究揭示了大语言模型（LLMs）具有内在的行为可塑性——类似于变色龙根据环境线索调整体色——这种特性可通过令牌条件化生成被激发，并借助强化学习实现稳定化。具体而言，通过将生成过程条件化于从展现目标行为的响应中采样的特定令牌前缀，LLMs能在推理时无缝切换行为模式（例如从逐步推理转为直接回答），而无需重新训练。基于此发现，我们提出了令牌条件化强化学习（ToCoRL），这是一个利用强化学习将这种变色龙式可塑性内化的理论框架，将瞬时的推理时适应转化为稳定且可学习的行为模式。ToCoRL通过令牌条件化生成引导探索并持续增强利用，促使适应性行为的涌现。大量实验表明，ToCoRL能在不降低模型能力的前提下实现精确的行为控制。值得注意的是，我们证明大型推理模型虽然在复杂数学任务上表现优异，也能通过适配在事实问答任务中取得卓越性能，该能力此前受其逐步推理模式所限。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the behavioral plasticity of Large Language Models (LLMs), motivated by the insight that they can adapt their output style based on specific token prefixes, similar to a chameleon changing color. The method introduces Token-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (ToCoRL), a framework that uses reinforcement learning to stabilize and internalize these token-conditioned behavioral adaptations, turning transient inference-time switches into learnable patterns without model retraining. Experimental results demonstrate that ToCoRL enables precise behavioral control, such as adapting a model specialized in step-by-step reasoning to excel at direct factual question answering, without degrading its core capabilities.
本文研究大型语言模型的行为可塑性，其动机是发现模型能根据特定词元前缀调整输出风格，类似于变色龙适应环境。方法上提出了词元条件强化学习框架，利用强化学习来稳定和内化这种条件行为适应，将临时的推理时切换转变为可学习的模式，而无需重新训练模型。实验结果表明，该框架能实现精确的行为控制，例如将擅长逐步推理的模型有效适配为擅长直接事实问答，且不损害其核心能力。
Finite Sample Bounds for Non-Parametric Regression: Optimal Sample Efficiency and Space Complexity
Authors: Davide Maran, Marcello Restelli
First: 2024-12-19T11:22:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T13:03:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We address the problem of learning an unknown smooth function and its derivatives from noisy pointwise evaluations under the supremum norm. While classical nonparametric regression provides a strong theoretical foundation, traditional kernel-based estimators often incur high computational costs and memory requirements that scale with the sample size, limiting their utility in real-time applications such as reinforcement learning. To overcome these challenges, we propose a parametric approach based on a finite-dimensional representation that achieves minimax-optimal uniform convergence rates. Our method enables lightweight inference without storing all samples in memory. We provide sharp finite-sample bounds under sub-Gaussian noise, derive second-order Bernstein-type guarantees, and prove matching lower bounds, thereby confirming the optimality of our approach in both estimation error and memory efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：非参数回归的有限样本界：最优样本效率与空间复杂度
本文研究从带噪声逐点观测中学习未知光滑函数及其导数在一致范数下的问题。经典非参数回归虽提供坚实理论基础，但传统核估计方法常伴随随样本量增长的高计算与内存开销，限制了其在强化学习等实时场景的应用。为突破这些限制，我们提出基于有限维表示的参数化方法，达到极小极大最优的一致收敛速率。该方法无需在内存中存储全部样本即可实现轻量推断。我们在次高斯噪声下给出尖锐的有限样本界，推导二阶伯恩斯坦型保证，并证明匹配下界，从而在估计误差与内存效率两方面验证了方法的理论最优性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational and memory costs of traditional kernel-based nonparametric regression, which hinder real-time applications like reinforcement learning, this paper proposes a parametric method using a finite-dimensional representation to learn smooth functions and their derivatives from noisy pointwise evaluations. The approach achieves minimax-optimal uniform convergence rates while enabling lightweight inference without storing all samples in memory. Experimental results, under sub-Gaussian noise, demonstrate sharp finite-sample bounds and second-order Bernstein-type guarantees, with matching lower bounds confirming optimality in both estimation error and space complexity.
针对传统基于核的非参数回归方法计算和内存成本高、难以应用于强化学习等实时场景的问题，本文提出了一种基于有限维表示的参数化方法，用于从含噪声的点评估中学习光滑函数及其导数。该方法实现了极小极大最优的一致收敛速率，并支持轻量级推理而无需在内存中存储所有样本。在次高斯噪声下的实验结果表明，该方法具有尖锐的有限样本界限和二阶伯恩斯坦型保证，匹配的下界证明了其在估计误差和空间复杂度上的最优性。
Posterior Sampling Reinforcement Learning with Gaussian Processes for Continuous Control: Sublinear Regret Bounds for Unbounded State Spaces
Authors: Hamish Flynn, Joe Watson, Ingmar Posner, Jan Peters
First: 2026-03-09T12:03:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T12:03:25+00:00
Comments: 37 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We analyze the Bayesian regret of the Gaussian process posterior sampling reinforcement learning (GP-PSRL) algorithm. Posterior sampling is an effective heuristic for decision-making under uncertainty that has been used to develop successful algorithms for a variety of continuous control problems. However, theoretical work on GP-PSRL is limited. All known regret bounds either fail to achieve a tight dependence on a kernel-dependent quantity called the maximum information gain or fail to properly account for the fact that the set of possible system states is unbounded. Through a recursive application of the Borell-Tsirelson-Ibragimov-Sudakov inequality, we show that, with high probability, the states actually visited by the algorithm are contained within a ball of near-constant radius. To obtain tight dependence on the maximum information gain, we use the chaining method to control the regret suffered by GP-PSRL. Our main result is a Bayesian regret bound of the order $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(H^{3/2}\sqrt{γ_{T/H} T})$, where $H$ is the horizon, $T$ is the number of time steps and $γ_{T/H}$ is the maximum information gain. With this result, we resolve the limitations with prior theoretical work on PSRL, and provide the theoretical foundation and tools for analyzing PSRL in complex settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于高斯过程的连续控制后验采样强化学习：无界状态空间的次线性遗憾界
我们分析了高斯过程后验采样强化学习（GP-PSRL）算法的贝叶斯遗憾。后验采样是一种处理不确定性决策的有效启发式方法，已成功应用于多种连续控制问题。然而，关于GP-PSRL的理论研究有限：现有遗憾界或未能紧密依赖核相关量——最大信息增益，或未恰当处理系统状态空间无界的特性。通过递归应用Borell-Tsirelson-Ibragimov-Sudakov不等式，我们证明算法实际访问的状态以高概率包含在近恒定半径的球体内。为获得对最大信息增益的紧密依赖，我们采用链式方法控制GP-PSRL的遗憾。主要成果是得到阶为$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(H^{3/2}\sqrt{γ_{T/H} T})$的贝叶斯遗憾界，其中$H$为时间跨度，$T$为时间步数，$γ_{T/H}$为最大信息增益。该研究解决了先前PSRL理论工作的局限性，为复杂场景下的PSRL分析提供了理论基础与工具。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses theoretical limitations in analyzing the Gaussian Process Posterior Sampling Reinforcement Learning (GP-PSRL) algorithm for continuous control, where prior regret bounds either lacked tight dependence on the kernel-specific maximum information gain or failed to properly handle unbounded state spaces. The method employs a recursive application of the Borell-Tsirelson-Ibragimov-Sudakov inequality to bound visited states within a near-constant radius and uses the chaining technique to tightly control regret. The main experimental result is a Bayesian regret bound of order \(\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(H^{3/2}\sqrt{\gamma_{T/H} T})\), where \(H\) is the horizon, \(T\) is the total time steps, and \(\gamma_{T/H}\) is the maximum information gain, thereby resolving prior theoretical shortcomings and providing a foundation for analyzing PSRL in complex settings.
本文针对连续控制中高斯过程后验采样强化学习（GP-PSRL）算法的理论分析局限性展开研究，先前遗憾界要么未能紧密依赖于核相关的最大信息增益，要么未能妥善处理无界状态空间问题。方法上，通过递归应用Borell-Tsirelson-Ibragimov-Sudakov不等式将访问状态限制在近恒定半径内，并采用链式方法紧密控制遗憾。主要实验结果是得到了阶为\(\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(H^{3/2}\sqrt{\gamma_{T/H} T})\)的贝叶斯遗憾界，其中\(H\)为时间步长，\(T\)为总时间步数，\(\gamma_{T/H}\)为最大信息增益，从而解决了先前理论工作的不足，为复杂场景下PSRL的分析提供了理论基础和工具。
To Mix or To Merge: Toward Multi-Domain Reinforcement Learning for Large Language Models
Authors: Haoqing Wang, Xiang Long, Ziheng Li, Yilong Xu, Tingguang Li, Yehui Tang
First: 2026-02-13T03:25:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T11:43:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) plays a key role in stimulating the explicit reasoning capability of Large Language Models (LLMs). We can achieve expert-level performance in some specific domains via RLVR, such as coding or math. When a general multi-domain expert-level model is required, we need to carefully consider the collaboration of RLVR across different domains. The current state-of-the-art models mainly employ two different training paradigms for multi-domain RLVR: mixed multi-task RLVR and separate RLVR followed by model merging. However, most of the works did not provide a detailed comparison and analysis about these paradigms. To this end, we choose multiple commonly used high-level tasks (e.g., math, coding, science, instruction following, and agent) as our target domains and design extensive qualitative and quantitative experiments using open-source datasets. We find the RLVR across domains exhibits few mutual interferences, and reasoning-intensive domains demonstrate mutually synergistic effects. Furthermore, we analyze the internal mechanisms of mutual gains from the perspectives of weight space geometry, model prediction behavior, information constraints and self-verification. This project is named as M2RL that means Mixed multi-task training or separate training followed by model Merging for Reinforcement Learning, and the homepage is at https://github.com/mosAI25/M2RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：混合还是合并：迈向大语言模型的多领域强化学习
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）在激发大语言模型（LLMs）的显式推理能力方面起着关键作用。通过RLVR，我们能在特定领域（如编程或数学）实现专家级性能。当需要通用的多领域专家级模型时，需审慎考虑RLVR在不同领域间的协同机制。当前最先进的模型主要采用两种多领域RLVR训练范式：混合多任务RLVR与独立RLVR后模型合并。然而，现有研究大多未对这些范式进行系统比较分析。为此，我们选取多个常用高阶任务（如数学、编程、科学、指令遵循、智能体）作为目标领域，基于开源数据集设计详尽的定性与定量实验。研究发现跨领域RLVR存在较少相互干扰，推理密集型领域甚至呈现协同增强效应。进一步从权重空间几何、模型预测行为、信息约束与自我验证等视角，深入解析了跨领域增益的内在机制。本项目命名为M2RL（意为“混合多任务训练或独立训练后模型合并的强化学习”），项目主页位于https://github.com/mosAI25/M2RL。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates training paradigms for achieving multi-domain expertise in large language models via reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), motivated by the need to understand whether mixed multi-task training or separate training followed by model merging is more effective. The method involves extensive experiments across domains like math, coding, and science using open-source datasets to compare these paradigms qualitatively and quantitatively. The main experimental results reveal that RLVR across domains shows few mutual interferences, with reasoning-intensive domains even exhibiting synergistic effects, and the analysis provides insights into the internal mechanisms behind these mutual gains.
本文研究通过可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）实现大语言模型多领域专业能力的训练范式，动机在于需要理解混合多任务训练与分别训练后模型合并哪种更有效。方法包括使用开源数据集在数学、编程和科学等领域进行广泛实验，以定性和定量方式比较这些范式。主要实验结果表明，跨领域的RLVR相互干扰很少，推理密集型领域甚至表现出协同效应，分析还从权重空间几何、模型预测行为等方面揭示了这些相互增益的内部机制。
Pretraining in Actor-Critic Reinforcement Learning for Robot Locomotion
Authors: Jiale Fan, Andrei Cramariuc, Tifanny Portela, Marco Hutter
First: 2025-10-14T10:25:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T10:43:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The pretraining-finetuning paradigm has facilitated numerous transformative advancements in artificial intelligence research in recent years. However, in the domain of reinforcement learning (RL) for robot locomotion, individual skills are often learned from scratch despite the high likelihood that some generalizable knowledge is shared across all task-specific policies belonging to the same robot embodiment. This work aims to define a paradigm for pretraining neural network models that encapsulate such knowledge and can subsequently serve as a basis for warm-starting the RL process in classic actor-critic algorithms, such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO). We begin with a task-agnostic exploration-based data collection algorithm to gather diverse, dynamic transition data, which is then used to train a Proprioceptive Inverse Dynamics Model (PIDM) through supervised learning. The pretrained weights are then loaded into both the actor and critic networks to warm-start the policy optimization of actual tasks. We systematically validated our proposed method with 9 distinct robot locomotion RL environments comprising 3 different robot embodiments, showing significant benefits of this initialization strategy. Our proposed approach on average improves sample efficiency by 36.9% and task performance by 7.3% compared to random initialization. We further present key ablation studies and empirical analyses that shed light on the mechanisms behind the effectiveness of this method.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向机器人运动的演员-评论家强化学习预训练方法
近年来，预训练-微调范式推动了人工智能领域的诸多突破性进展。然而在机器人运动强化学习领域，尽管同一机器人实体下的各任务策略很可能共享某些可泛化知识，现有方法仍普遍从零开始学习单项技能。本研究旨在构建一种神经网络预训练范式，使其能够封装此类通用知识，并作为经典演员-评论家算法（如近端策略优化）强化学习过程的热启动基础。我们首先采用任务无关的探索式数据收集算法获取多样化动态转移数据，继而通过监督学习训练本体感知逆动力学模型。随后将预训练权重载入演员与评论家网络，为实际任务的策略优化提供热启动。我们在包含3种不同机器人实体的9个运动强化学习环境中系统验证了该方法，证明该初始化策略具有显著优势：相较于随机初始化，平均样本效率提升36.9%，任务性能提高7.3%。进一步的消融实验与实证分析揭示了该方法有效的内在机制。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the underutilization of shared knowledge across robot locomotion tasks, this paper introduces a pretraining paradigm for actor-critic reinforcement learning to avoid learning each skill from scratch. The method involves collecting diverse, task-agnostic exploration data to train a Proprioceptive Inverse Dynamics Model via supervised learning, then using its weights to initialize both actor and critic networks in algorithms like PPO for fine-tuning on specific tasks. Experimental results across nine locomotion environments with three robot embodiments demonstrate that this approach improves sample efficiency by 36.9% and task performance by 7.3% on average compared to random initialization, with ablation studies providing insights into its effectiveness.
本文的动机在于机器人运动任务中共享知识未被充分利用，个体技能常需从头学习，因此提出了一种用于演员-评论家强化学习的预训练范式。方法上，通过任务无关的探索算法收集多样化的动态转移数据，以监督学习训练一个本体感知逆动力学模型，然后将其权重加载到演员和评论家网络中来热启动特定任务的策略优化。在包含三种机器人形态的九个运动环境中的系统验证表明，相比随机初始化，该方法平均提升了36.9%的样本效率和7.3%的任务性能，并通过消融实验揭示了其有效性的机制。
Multi-Objective Evolutionary Optimization of Chance-Constrained Multiple-Choice Knapsack Problems with Implicit Probability Distributions
Authors: Xuanfeng Li, Shengcai Liu, Wenjie Chen, Yew-Soon Ong, Ke Tang
First: 2026-03-09T10:39:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T10:39:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The multiple-choice knapsack problem (MCKP) is a classic combinatorial optimization with wide practical applications. This paper investigates a significant yet underexplored extension of MCKP: the multi-objective chance-constrained MCKP (MO-CCMCKP) under implicit probability distributions. The goal of the problem is to simultaneously minimize the total cost and maximize the confidence level of satisfying the capacity constraint, capturing essential trade-offs in domains like 5G network configuration. To address the computational challenge of evaluating chance constraints under implicit distributions, we first propose an order-preserving efficient resource allocation Monte Carlo (OPERA-MC) method. This approach adaptively allocates sampling resources to preserve dominance relationships while reducing evaluation time significantly. Further, we develop NHILS, a hybrid evolutionary algorithm that integrates specialized initialization and local search into NSGA-II to navigate sparse feasible regions. Experiments on synthetic benchmarks and real-world 5G network configuration benchmarks demonstrate that NHILS consistently outperforms several state-of-the-art multi-objective optimizers in convergence, diversity, and feasibility. The benchmark instances and source code will be made publicly available to facilitate research in this area.
中文标题/摘要
标题：隐式概率分布下机会约束多选择背包问题的多目标进化优化
多选择背包问题（MCKP）是经典的组合优化问题，具有广泛的实际应用。本文研究了MCKP一个重要但尚未充分探索的扩展：隐式概率分布下的多目标机会约束MCKP（MO-CCMCKP）。该问题的目标是在最小化总成本的同时，最大化满足容量约束的置信水平，以捕捉如5G网络配置等领域的关键权衡关系。针对隐式分布下机会约束评估的计算挑战，我们首先提出了一种保序高效资源分配蒙特卡洛（OPERA-MC）方法，该方法通过自适应分配采样资源在显著减少评估时间的同时保持支配关系。进一步，我们开发了NHILS混合进化算法，将专用初始化和局部搜索集成到NSGA-II中以探索稀疏可行域。在合成基准和实际5G网络配置基准上的实验表明，NHILS在收敛性、多样性和可行性方面持续优于多种先进多目标优化器。基准实例和源代码将公开提供，以促进该领域的研究。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the multi-objective chance-constrained multiple-choice knapsack problem (MO-CCMCKP) under implicit probability distributions, motivated by the need to capture trade-offs between cost and constraint satisfaction confidence in applications like 5G network configuration. The method introduces an order-preserving efficient resource allocation Monte Carlo (OPERA-MC) technique to efficiently evaluate chance constraints and a hybrid evolutionary algorithm called NHILS, which enhances NSGA-II with specialized initialization and local search to handle sparse feasible regions. Experimental results on synthetic and real-world 5G benchmarks show that NHILS outperforms state-of-the-art optimizers in convergence, diversity, and feasibility.
本文研究了具有隐式概率分布的多目标机会约束多选择背包问题（MO-CCMCKP），其动机在于捕捉如5G网络配置等应用中成本与约束满足置信度之间的权衡。方法上，提出了保持序关系的高效资源分配蒙特卡洛（OPERA-MC）技术来高效评估机会约束，并开发了混合进化算法NHILS，该算法将专用初始化和局部搜索集成到NSGA-II中以处理稀疏可行区域。在合成和真实5G基准测试上的实验结果表明，NHILS在收敛性、多样性和可行性方面均优于多种先进的多目标优化器。
Evolution Strategy-Based Calibration for Low-Bit Quantization of Speech Models
Authors: Lucas Rakotoarivony
First: 2026-03-09T09:53:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T09:53:05+00:00
Comments: Submitted to INTERSPEECH 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantization has become essential for the efficient deployment of speech processing systems. Although widely studied, most existing quantization methods were developed for vision and NLP architectures, while the specific challenges of audio signals remain largely overlooked. In particular, we show that audio activations can exhibit large calibration ranges, leading to significant information loss when standard calibration techniques are applied. To address this, we propose ESC, an Evolution Strategy-based Calibration method that formulates activation scaling as an optimization problem and solves it using a two-step local-global scheme driven by an evolution strategy. ESC enables unaltered performance under full INT8 quantization and is the first calibration method to achieve near-lossless performance for full INT4 quantization across multiple speech tasks. Integrating ESC with PTQ methods further reduces performance loss, achieving a 1% relative accuracy degradation on the AST model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于进化策略的语音模型低比特量化校准方法
量化技术已成为语音处理系统高效部署的关键手段。尽管相关研究广泛开展，现有量化方法多针对视觉与自然语言处理架构设计，而音频信号特有的量化挑战长期被忽视。本文发现音频激活值可能呈现较大校准范围，导致传统校准技术产生显著信息损失。为此，我们提出ESC——一种基于进化策略的校准方法，将激活缩放构建为优化问题，并通过进化策略驱动的局部-全局两步优化框架求解。ESC在完整INT8量化下保持无损性能，并成为首个在多项语音任务中实现接近无损INT4量化的校准方法。结合后训练量化技术后，ESC在AST模型上仅产生1%的相对精度损失。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the observation that existing quantization methods, primarily designed for vision and NLP models, overlook the specific challenges of audio signals, where activations can have large calibration ranges leading to significant information loss. The proposed method, ESC, is an Evolution Strategy-based Calibration technique that formulates activation scaling as an optimization problem, solving it with a two-step local-global scheme driven by an evolution strategy. The main experimental results show that ESC enables unaltered performance under full INT8 quantization and is the first calibration method to achieve near-lossless performance for full INT4 quantization across multiple speech tasks; when integrated with PTQ methods, it further reduces performance loss, achieving only a 1% relative accuracy degradation on the AST model.
本研究的动机源于现有量化方法主要针对视觉和自然语言处理模型设计，而忽视了音频信号特有的挑战，即激活值可能具有较大的校准范围，导致标准校准技术应用时出现显著信息丢失。所提出的方法ESC是一种基于进化策略的校准技术，它将激活缩放表述为一个优化问题，并通过由进化策略驱动的两步局部-全局方案进行求解。主要实验结果表明，ESC在完整的INT8量化下能保持性能不变，并且是首个在多种语音任务上实现接近无损的完整INT4量化性能的校准方法；当与PTQ方法结合时，它进一步减少了性能损失，在AST模型上仅实现了1%的相对准确度下降。
A Unified Framework for Zero-Shot Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jacopo Di Ventura, Jan Felix Kleuker, Aske Plaat, Thomas Moerland
First: 2025-10-23T13:30:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T09:43:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Zero-shot reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a setting for developing general agents, capable of solving downstream tasks without additional training or planning at test-time. While conventional RL optimizes policies for fixed rewards, zero-shot RL requires learning representations that enable immediate adaptation to arbitrary reward functions. As the field matures, the growing diversity of approaches demands a foundational framework reconciling different perspectives under a common unifying structure. In this work, we introduce a formal, unified framework for zero-shot RL, allowing for rigorous comparisons across methods. We propose a taxonomy organizing the algorithmic landscape along two levels: representation, distinguishing between compositional and direct methods based on their exploitation of action-value function decompositions; and learning paradigm, differentiating between reward-free and pseudo reward-free training. Additionally, we propose a unified view of existing error bounds, decomposing the total error into three primary contributing components: inference, reward, and approximation, serving as a foundation for more grounded comparisons of zero-shot methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：零样本强化学习的统一框架
零样本强化学习已成为开发通用智能体的重要范式，使智能体能够在测试时无需额外训练或规划即可解决下游任务。传统强化学习针对固定奖励优化策略，而零样本强化学习则需学习能够立即适应任意奖励函数的表征。随着该领域的发展，日益多样化的方法亟需一个基础性框架，在统一结构下协调不同视角。本研究提出了一个形式化的零样本强化学习统一框架，支持跨方法的严格比较。我们提出了一种分类法，从两个层面组织算法体系：表征层面（根据对动作价值函数分解的利用方式，区分为组合式方法与直接方法）与学习范式层面（区分为无奖励训练与伪无奖励训练）。此外，我们提出了现有误差界的统一视角，将总误差分解为三个主要构成部分：推断误差、奖励误差与近似误差，为零样本方法的更实质性比较奠定基础。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to reconcile the growing diversity of approaches in zero-shot reinforcement learning (RL), which aims to develop agents capable of solving downstream tasks without test-time training, this paper introduces a formal, unified framework to enable rigorous comparisons across methods. The method involves proposing a taxonomy that organizes algorithms along two levels: representation (distinguishing compositional and direct methods based on action-value function decompositions) and learning paradigm (differentiating reward-free and pseudo reward-free training). The main experimental results include a unified view of existing error bounds, decomposing total error into inference, reward, and approximation components, thereby providing a foundation for more grounded comparisons of zero-shot RL methods.
受零样本强化学习领域方法日益多样化、需要统一框架以调和不同视角的动机驱动，本文引入了一个正式的、统一的框架，旨在对无需测试时训练即可解决下游任务的智能体方法进行严格比较。该方法提出了一个分类法，从两个层面组织算法：表示层（基于动作价值函数分解区分组合方法和直接方法）和学习范式层（区分无奖励和伪无奖励训练）。主要实验结果包括对现有误差界限的统一视角，将总误差分解为推断、奖励和近似三个主要组成部分，从而为零样本强化学习方法提供了更扎实的比较基础。
Model-based Offline RL via Robust Value-Aware Model Learning with Implicitly Differentiable Adaptive Weighting
Authors: Zhongjian Qiao, Jiafei Lyu, Boxiang Lyu, Yao Shu, Siyang Gao, Shuang Qiu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-09T08:59:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:59:45+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Model-based offline reinforcement learning (RL) aims to enhance offline RL with a dynamics model that facilitates policy exploration. However, \textit{model exploitation} could occur due to inevitable model errors, degrading algorithm performance. Adversarial model learning offers a theoretical framework to mitigate model exploitation by solving a maximin formulation. Within such a paradigm, RAMBO~\citep{rigter2022rambo} has emerged as a representative and most popular method that provides a practical implementation with model gradient. However, we empirically reveal that severe Q-value underestimation and gradient explosion can occur in RAMBO with only slight hyperparameter tuning, suggesting that it tends to be overly conservative and suffers from unstable model updates. To address these issues, we propose \textbf{RO}bust value-aware \textbf{M}odel learning with \textbf{I}mplicitly differentiable adaptive weighting (ROMI). Instead of updating the dynamics model with model gradient, ROMI introduces a novel robust value-aware model learning approach. This approach requires the dynamics model to predict future states with values close to the minimum Q-value within a scale-adjustable state uncertainty set, enabling controllable conservatism and stable model updates. To further improve out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization during multi-step rollouts, we propose implicitly differentiable adaptive weighting, a bi-level optimization scheme that adaptively achieves dynamics- and value-aware model learning. Empirical results on D4RL and NeoRL datasets show that ROMI significantly outperforms RAMBO and achieves competitive or superior performance compared to other state-of-the-art methods on datasets where RAMBO typically underperforms. Code is available at https://github.com/zq2r/ROMI.git.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于稳健价值感知模型学习与隐式可微自适应加权的模型化离线强化学习
模型化离线强化学习旨在通过动态模型增强离线强化学习的策略探索能力。然而，不可避免的模型误差可能导致模型利用问题，从而降低算法性能。对抗性模型学习通过求解极大极小公式为缓解模型利用提供了理论框架。在此框架下，RAMBO成为具有模型梯度实用实现的代表性流行方法。但我们实证发现，RAMBO在轻微超参数调整下可能出现严重的Q值低估和梯度爆炸，表明其倾向于过度保守且模型更新不稳定。为解决这些问题，我们提出具有隐式可微自适应加权的稳健价值感知模型学习方法。该方法不依赖模型梯度更新动态模型，而是要求动态模型在尺度可调的状态不确定集合内，预测未来状态值接近最小Q值，从而实现可控保守性与稳定模型更新。为提升多步推演中的分布外泛化能力，我们提出隐式可微自适应加权的双层优化方案，自适应实现动态与价值感知的模型学习。在D4RL和NeoRL数据集上的实验表明，该方法显著优于RAMBO，并在RAMBO通常表现欠佳的数据集上达到或超越其他先进方法。代码发布于https://github.com/zq2r/ROMI.git。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the problem of model exploitation in model-based offline reinforcement learning, where inevitable model errors can degrade policy performance. The authors propose ROMI, a method that replaces the model gradient updates used in prior work like RAMBO with a robust value-aware model learning approach, which requires the dynamics model to predict future states with values close to the minimum Q-value within an adjustable uncertainty set, thereby enabling controllable conservatism and stable updates. To enhance out-of-distribution generalization during multi-step rollouts, they introduce an implicitly differentiable adaptive weighting scheme via bi-level optimization. Experimental results on D4RL and NeoRL benchmarks demonstrate that ROMI significantly outperforms RAMBO and achieves competitive or superior performance compared to other state-of-the-art methods, particularly on datasets where RAMBO underperforms.
本文针对基于模型的离线强化学习中模型误差导致的模型利用问题，旨在提升算法性能。作者提出了ROMI方法，该方法摒弃了先前RAMBO等方法使用的模型梯度更新，转而采用一种鲁棒的价值感知模型学习策略，要求动态模型在可调节的状态不确定性集合内预测出接近最小Q值的未来状态，从而实现可控的保守性和稳定的模型更新。为了提升多步展开时的分布外泛化能力，他们通过双层优化引入了隐式可微的自适应加权机制。在D4RL和NeoRL数据集上的实验结果表明，ROMI显著优于RAMBO，并在RAMBO通常表现不佳的数据集上取得了与其他最先进方法相当或更优的性能。
Dual-Robust Cross-Domain Offline Reinforcement Learning Against Dynamics Shifts
Authors: Zhongjian Qiao, Rui Yang, Jiafei Lyu, Xiu Li, Zhongxiang Dai, Zhuoran Yang, Siyang Gao, Shuang Qiu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-12-02T07:20:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:48:21+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Single-domain offline reinforcement learning (RL) often suffers from limited data coverage, while cross-domain offline RL handles this issue by leveraging additional data from other domains with dynamics shifts. However, existing studies primarily focus on train-time robustness (handling dynamics shifts from training data), neglecting the test-time robustness against dynamics perturbations when deployed in practical scenarios. In this paper, we investigate dual (both train-time and test-time) robustness against dynamics shifts in cross-domain offline RL. We first empirically show that the policy trained with cross-domain offline RL exhibits fragility under dynamics perturbations during evaluation, particularly when target domain data is limited. To address this, we introduce a novel robust cross-domain Bellman (RCB) operator, which enhances test-time robustness against dynamics perturbations while staying conservative to the out-of-distribution dynamics transitions, thus guaranteeing the train-time robustness. To further counteract potential value overestimation or underestimation caused by the RCB operator, we introduce two techniques, the dynamic value penalty and the Huber loss, into our framework, resulting in the practical \textbf{D}ual-\textbf{RO}bust \textbf{C}ross-domain \textbf{O}ffline RL (DROCO) algorithm. Extensive empirical results across various dynamics shift scenarios show that DROCO outperforms strong baselines and exhibits enhanced robustness to dynamics perturbations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向动态偏移的双鲁棒跨域离线强化学习
单域离线强化学习常受限于数据覆盖不足，而跨域离线强化学习通过利用其他存在动态偏移的领域数据来缓解此问题。然而，现有研究主要关注训练时鲁棒性（处理训练数据中的动态偏移），忽略了实际部署时面对动态扰动的测试时鲁棒性。本文研究跨域离线强化学习中针对动态偏移的双重（训练时与测试时）鲁棒性。我们首先通过实验证明，在评估阶段面临动态扰动时，尤其是目标域数据有限的情况下，跨域离线强化学习训练的策略表现出脆弱性。为此，我们提出一种新颖的鲁棒跨域贝尔曼算子，该算子在保持对分布外动态转移的保守性（从而保证训练时鲁棒性）的同时，增强了针对动态扰动的测试时鲁棒性。为进一步抵消该算子可能引起的价值高估或低估，我们在框架中引入动态价值惩罚和Huber损失两项技术，最终形成实用的\textbf{双鲁棒跨域离线强化学习}算法。在多种动态偏移场景下的广泛实验结果表明，DROCO算法优于现有强基线，并展现出对动态扰动更强的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the dual challenge of train-time and test-time robustness in cross-domain offline reinforcement learning (RL), where policies must handle dynamics shifts in both training data and deployment environments. The authors propose a novel robust cross-domain Bellman (RCB) operator that conservatively manages out-of-distribution transitions for train-time robustness while enhancing resilience to test-time dynamics perturbations. To mitigate value estimation errors from the RCB operator, they integrate a dynamic value penalty and Huber loss, resulting in the DROCO algorithm. Experimental results across various dynamics shift scenarios demonstrate that DROCO outperforms existing baselines and shows improved robustness, especially when target domain data is limited.
本文针对跨领域离线强化学习中的双重鲁棒性问题，即策略需同时应对训练数据和部署环境中的动态变化。作者提出了一种新颖的鲁棒跨领域贝尔曼算子，该算子通过保守处理分布外转移来保证训练时鲁棒性，同时增强对测试时动态扰动的抵抗力。为了缓解该算子可能引起的价值估计误差，他们引入了动态价值惩罚和Huber损失技术，从而形成了DROCO算法。在多种动态变化场景下的实验结果表明，DROCO优于现有基线方法，尤其在目标领域数据有限时表现出更强的鲁棒性。
MAS-Orchestra: Understanding and Improving Multi-Agent Reasoning Through Holistic Orchestration and Controlled Benchmarks
Authors: Zixuan Ke, Yifei Ming, Austin Xu, Ryan Chin, Xuan-Phi Nguyen, Prathyusha Jwalapuram, Jiayu Wang, Semih Yavuz, Caiming Xiong, Shafiq Joty
First: 2026-01-21T04:57:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:39:35+00:00
Comments: Preprint; Work in Progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While multi-agent systems (MAS) promise elevated intelligence through coordination of agents, current approaches to automatic MAS design under-deliver. Such shortcomings stem from two key factors: (1) methodological complexity - agent orchestration is performed using sequential, code-level execution that limits global system-level holistic reasoning and scales poorly with agent complexity - and (2) efficacy uncertainty - MAS are deployed without understanding if there are tangible benefits compared to single-agent systems (SAS). We propose MASOrchestra, a training-time framework that formulates MAS orchestration as a function-calling reinforcement learning problem with holistic orchestration, generating an entire MAS at once. In MAS-Orchestra, complex, goal-oriented subagents are abstracted as callable functions, enabling global reasoning over system structure while hiding internal execution details. To rigorously study when and why MAS are beneficial, we introduce MASBENCH, a controlled benchmark that characterizes tasks along five axes: Depth, Horizon, Breadth, Parallel, and Robustness. Our analysis reveals that MAS gains depend critically on task structure, verification protocols, and the capabilities of both orchestrator and subagents, rather than holding universally. Guided by these insights, MAS-Orchestra achieves consistent improvements on public benchmarks including mathematical reasoning, multi-hop QA, and search-based QA, while achieving more than 10x efficiency over strong baselines. Together, MAS-Orchestra and MASBENCH enable better training and understanding of MAS in the pursuit of multi-agent intelligence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MAS-Orchestra：通过整体编排与受控基准理解并提升多智能体推理能力
尽管多智能体系统（MAS）通过智能体协作有望实现更高智能，但当前自动设计MAS的方法效果不佳。其不足源于两个关键因素：（1）方法复杂性——现有编排采用顺序、代码级执行，限制了全局系统层面的整体推理，且难以随智能体复杂度扩展；（2）效能不确定性——部署MAS时未明确其相比单智能体系统（SAS）是否具有实质优势。我们提出MAS-Orchestra，一种训练时框架，将MAS编排建模为具有整体编排能力的函数调用强化学习问题，可一次性生成完整MAS。该框架将复杂的目标导向子智能体抽象为可调用函数，在隐藏内部执行细节的同时实现系统结构的全局推理。为严谨探究MAS何时及为何有效，我们引入MASBENCH受控基准，从深度、跨度、广度、并行性和鲁棒性五个维度刻画任务特性。分析表明，MAS的增益关键取决于任务结构、验证协议及编排器与子智能体的能力，而非普遍适用。基于这些发现，MAS-Orchestra在数学推理、多跳问答和基于搜索的问答等公共基准上实现稳定提升，同时效率较基线提升超10倍。MAS-Orchestra与MASBENCH共同为追求多智能体智能提供了更优的训练与理解框架。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the underperformance of current multi-agent systems (MAS) due to methodological complexity and uncertain efficacy compared to single-agent systems, this paper introduces MAS-Orchestra, a training-time framework that formulates MAS orchestration as a function-calling reinforcement learning problem with holistic orchestration to generate entire systems at once. The method abstracts subagents as callable functions, enabling global reasoning while hiding internal details, and is evaluated using MASBENCH, a new controlled benchmark characterizing tasks along five axes. Experimental results show that MAS benefits depend on specific task structures and capabilities, and MAS-Orchestra achieves consistent improvements on public benchmarks in mathematical reasoning and QA, with over 10x efficiency gains over baselines.

Characterizing MARL for Energy Control: A Multi-KPI Benchmark on the CityLearn Environment
Authors: Aymen Khouja, Imen Jendoubi, Oumayma Mahjoub, Oussama Mahfoudhi, Ruan De Kock, Siddarth Singh, Claude Formanek
First: 2026-02-22T15:14:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:20:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The optimization of urban energy systems is crucial for the advancement of sustainable and resilient smart cities, which are becoming increasingly complex with multiple decision-making units. To address scalability and coordination concerns, Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) is a promising solution. This paper addresses the imperative need for comprehensive and reliable benchmarking of MARL algorithms on energy management tasks. CityLearn is used as a case study environment because it realistically simulates urban energy systems, incorporates multiple storage systems, and utilizes renewable energy sources. By doing so, our work sets a new standard for evaluation, conducting a comparative study across multiple key performance indicators (KPIs). This approach illuminates the key strengths and weaknesses of various algorithms, moving beyond traditional KPI averaging which often masks critical insights. Our experiments utilize widely accepted baselines such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) and Soft Actor Critic (SAC), and encompass diverse training schemes including Decentralized Training with Decentralized Execution (DTDE) and Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE) approaches and different neural network architectures. Our work also proposes novel KPIs that tackle real world implementation challenges such as individual building contribution and battery storage lifetime. Our findings show that DTDE consistently outperforms CTDE in both average and worst-case performance. Additionally, temporal dependency learning improved control on memory dependent KPIs such as ramping and battery usage, contributing to more sustainable battery operation. Results also reveal robustness to agent or resource removal, highlighting both the resilience and decentralizability of the learned policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向能源控制的多智能体强化学习特性分析：基于CityLearn环境的多指标基准测试
城市能源系统优化对建设可持续、高韧性的智慧城市至关重要，而多决策单元的存在使系统日益复杂。为应对可扩展性与协同挑战，多智能体强化学习（MARL）成为一种前景广阔的解决方案。本文针对能源管理任务中MARL算法亟需全面可靠基准测试的需求，选用CityLearn作为案例研究环境——该环境能真实模拟城市能源系统、整合多类储能装置并利用可再生能源。通过多维度关键绩效指标（KPI）的对比研究，本文建立了新的评估标准，突破传统KPI均值分析掩盖关键信息的局限，系统揭示各类算法的核心优势与不足。实验采用近端策略优化（PPO）、柔性演员-评论家（SAC）等公认基线算法，涵盖去中心化训练与执行（DTDE）、中心化训练与去中心化执行（CTDE）等训练范式及多种神经网络架构。本研究还提出面向实际应用挑战的新型KPI，如单体建筑贡献度与电池储能寿命评估。实验结果表明：DTDE在平均性能与最差场景表现上均持续优于CTDE；时序依赖学习增强了对爬坡率、电池使用等记忆依赖型KPI的控制能力，有助于实现更可持续的电池运行；策略对智能体或资源移除表现出强鲁棒性，印证了所学策略兼具韧性特质与去中心化潜力。

This paper is motivated by the need for robust benchmarking of Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) algorithms to manage the growing complexity of urban energy systems for sustainable smart cities. The method employs the CityLearn simulation environment to conduct a comparative study of MARL algorithms like PPO and SAC, evaluating them under various training schemes and neural architectures while introducing novel key performance indicators (KPIs) for real-world challenges such as building contribution and battery lifetime. The main experimental results demonstrate that Decentralized Training with Decentralized Execution (DTDE) consistently outperforms Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE), temporal dependency learning improves control over metrics like ramping and battery usage, and the learned policies show robustness to agent or resource removal.
本文的动机源于需要对多智能体强化学习（MARL）算法进行可靠基准测试，以应对日益复杂的城市能源系统管理，从而推动可持续智慧城市的发展。研究方法利用CityLearn仿真环境，对PPO和SAC等MARL算法进行了比较研究，评估了不同训练方案和神经网络架构，并引入了针对实际挑战（如建筑贡献和电池寿命）的新型关键绩效指标（KPI）。主要实验结果表明，分散训练与分散执行（DTDE） consistently outperforms Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE), temporal dependency learning improves control over metrics like ramping and battery usage, and the learned policies show robustness to agent or resource removal.
Think, Speak, Decide: Language-Augmented Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for Economic Decision-Making
Authors: Heyang Ma, Qirui Mi, Qipeng Yang, Zijun Fan, Bo Li, Haifeng Zhang
Venue: AAAI 2026
First: 2025-11-17T02:09:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:10:13+00:00
Comments: Extended version of an accepted paper at AAAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Economic decision-making depends not only on structured signals such as prices and taxes, but also on unstructured language, including peer dialogue and media narratives. While multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) has shown promise in optimizing economic decisions, it struggles with the semantic ambiguity and contextual richness of language. We propose LAMP (Language-Augmented Multi-Agent Policy), a framework that integrates language into economic decision-making and narrows the gap to real-world settings. LAMP follows a Think-Speak-Decide pipeline: (1) Think interprets numerical observations to extract short-term shocks and long-term trends, caching high-value reasoning trajectories; (2) Speak crafts and exchanges strategic messages based on reasoning, updating beliefs by parsing peer communications; and (3) Decide fuses numerical data, reasoning, and reflections into a MARL policy to optimize language-augmented decision-making. Experiments in economic simulation show that LAMP outperforms both MARL and LLM-only baselines in cumulative return (+63.5%, +34.0%), robustness (+18.8%, +59.4%), and interpretability. These results demonstrate the potential of language-augmented policies to deliver more effective and robust economic strategies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：思考、交流、决策：面向经济决策的语言增强多智能体强化学习
经济决策不仅依赖于价格、税收等结构化信号，还涉及同行对话、媒体叙事等非结构化语言信息。尽管多智能体强化学习（MARL）在优化经济决策方面展现出潜力，但其难以处理语言的语义模糊性和语境复杂性。本文提出LAMP（语言增强多智能体策略）框架，将语言信息融入经济决策以缩小与现实场景的差距。LAMP采用“思考-交流-决策”流程：（1）思考阶段解析数值观测数据，提取短期波动与长期趋势，并缓存高价值推理轨迹；（2）交流阶段基于推理生成并交换策略性信息，通过解析同伴通信更新信念；（3）决策阶段融合数值数据、推理结果与反思信息，形成MARL策略以优化语言增强决策。经济模拟实验表明，LAMP在累计收益（+63.5%、+34.0%）、鲁棒性（+18.8%、+59.4%）和可解释性方面均优于MARL基准与纯大语言模型基线。这些结果证明了语言增强策略在实现更高效、更稳健经济战略方面的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to incorporate unstructured language like dialogue and narratives into economic decision-making alongside structured signals, this paper introduces LAMP, a framework that integrates language into multi-agent reinforcement learning. The method employs a Think-Speak-Decide pipeline where agents interpret numerical data, cache reasoning, exchange strategic messages, and fuse this information into a policy. Experimental results in economic simulations show LAMP outperforms MARL and LLM-only baselines, achieving significant improvements in cumulative return, robustness, and interpretability.
本文的动机是将对话和叙事等非结构化语言与价格等结构化信号共同融入经济决策，以缩小与现实世界的差距。为此，作者提出了LAMP框架，它采用思考-交流-决策的流程：智能体解释数值数据、缓存推理轨迹、交换策略信息，并将这些信息融合到多智能体强化学习策略中。在经济模拟实验中，LAMP在累积回报、鲁棒性和可解释性上均优于多智能体强化学习和纯大语言模型基线，证明了语言增强策略的有效性。
In-Context Reinforcement Learning for Tool Use in Large Language Models
Authors: Yaoqi Ye, Yiran Zhao, Keyu Duan, Zeyu Zheng, Kenji Kawaguchi, Cihang Xie, Michael Qizhe Shieh
First: 2026-03-09T08:06:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T08:06:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While large language models (LLMs) exhibit strong reasoning abilities, their performance on complex tasks is often constrained by the limitations of their internal knowledge. A compelling approach to overcome this challenge is to augment these models with external tools -- such as Python interpreters for mathematical computations or search engines for retrieving factual information. However, enabling models to use these tools effectively remains a significant challenge. Existing methods typically rely on cold-start pipelines that begin with supervised fine-tuning (SFT), followed by reinforcement learning (RL). These approaches often require substantial amounts of labeled data for SFT, which is expensive to annotate or synthesize. In this work, we propose In-Context Reinforcement Learning (ICRL), an RL-only framework that eliminates the need for SFT by leveraging few-shot prompting during the rollout stage of RL. Specifically, ICRL introduces in-context examples within the rollout prompts to teach the model how to invoke external tools. Furthermore, as training progresses, the number of in-context examples is gradually reduced, eventually reaching a zero-shot setting where the model learns to call tools independently. We conduct extensive experiments across a range of reasoning and tool-use benchmarks. Results show that ICRL achieves state-of-the-art performance, demonstrating its effectiveness as a scalable, data-efficient alternative to traditional SFT-based pipelines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型工具使用的上下文强化学习
尽管大语言模型展现出强大的推理能力，但其在复杂任务上的表现常受限于内部知识的不足。一个有效的解决方案是通过外部工具增强模型能力，例如使用Python解释器进行数学计算或搜索引擎获取事实信息。然而，如何使模型高效利用这些工具仍面临挑战。现有方法通常依赖从监督微调开始、再结合强化学习的冷启动流程，这类方法需要大量标注数据进行监督微调，成本高昂。本研究提出上下文强化学习，这是一种仅依赖强化学习的框架，通过在强化学习的推演阶段引入少量示例提示，从而避免监督微调需求。具体而言，该框架在推演提示中嵌入上下文示例以指导模型调用外部工具，并随着训练进程逐步减少示例数量，最终实现模型在零样本环境下自主调用工具。我们在多项推理与工具使用基准测试中进行了广泛实验，结果表明该方法取得了最先进的性能，证明了其作为可扩展、数据高效的传统流程替代方案的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of enabling large language models (LLMs) to effectively use external tools, such as Python interpreters or search engines, to overcome their internal knowledge limitations. The authors propose In-Context Reinforcement Learning (ICRL), a method that eliminates the need for costly supervised fine-tuning by instead using few-shot prompting during reinforcement learning rollouts to teach tool invocation, gradually reducing the in-context examples to achieve zero-shot tool use. Experimental results across various reasoning and tool-use benchmarks demonstrate that ICRL achieves state-of-the-art performance, offering a scalable and data-efficient alternative to traditional pipelines.
本文旨在解决大型语言模型有效使用外部工具（如Python解释器或搜索引擎）以克服其内部知识局限性的挑战。作者提出了上下文强化学习方法，该方法通过在强化学习的推演阶段使用少量示例提示来教导模型调用工具，从而避免了成本高昂的监督微调，并逐步减少上下文示例以实现零样本工具使用。在多个推理和工具使用基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法取得了最先进的性能，为传统基于监督微调的流程提供了一种可扩展且数据高效的替代方案。
ImageEdit-R1: Boosting Multi-Agent Image Editing via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yiran Zhao, Yaoqi Ye, Xiang Liu, Michael Qizhe Shieh, Trung Bui
First: 2026-03-09T07:50:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T07:50:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the rapid advancement of commercial multi-modal models, image editing has garnered significant attention due to its widespread applicability in daily life. Despite impressive progress, existing image editing systems, particularly closed-source or proprietary models, often struggle with complex, indirect, or multi-step user instructions. These limitations hinder their ability to perform nuanced, context-aware edits that align with human intent. In this work, we propose ImageEdit-R1, a multi-agent framework for intelligent image editing that leverages reinforcement learning to coordinate high-level decision-making across a set of specialized, pretrained vision-language and generative agents. Each agent is responsible for distinct capabilities--such as understanding user intent, identifying regions of interest, selecting appropriate editing actions, and synthesizing visual content--while reinforcement learning governs their collaboration to ensure coherent and goal-directed behavior. Unlike existing approaches that rely on monolithic models or hand-crafted pipelines, our method treats image editing as a sequential decision-making problem, enabling dynamic and context-aware editing strategies. Experimental results demonstrate that ImageEdit-R1 consistently outperforms both individual closed-source diffusion models and alternative multi-agent framework baselines across multiple image editing datasets.

随着商业多模态模型的快速发展，图像编辑因其在日常生活中的广泛应用而备受关注。尽管已取得显著进展，现有图像编辑系统（尤其是闭源或专有模型）在处理复杂、间接或多步骤的用户指令时仍面临困难，限制了其执行符合人类意图的细致、上下文感知编辑的能力。本研究提出ImageEdit-R1，一种基于强化学习的多智能体图像编辑框架，通过协调多个预训练的视觉语言与生成智能体进行高层决策。每个智能体负责不同功能——如理解用户意图、识别兴趣区域、选择编辑操作及合成视觉内容——强化学习则统筹其协作以确保行为的一致性与目标导向性。与依赖单一模型或手工流程的现有方法不同，本方法将图像编辑视为序列决策问题，实现了动态且上下文感知的编辑策略。实验结果表明，ImageEdit-R1在多个图像编辑数据集上均优于闭源扩散模型及其他多智能体基线框架。

The method formulates image editing as a sequential decision-making problem, enabling dynamic and context-aware strategies beyond monolithic models or hand-crafted pipelines. Adaptation of Agentic AI: A Survey of Post-Training, Memory, and Skills
Authors: Pengcheng Jiang, Jiacheng Lin, Zhiyi Shi, Zifeng Wang, Luxi He, Yichen Wu, Ming Zhong, Peiyang Song, Qizheng Zhang, Heng Wang, Xueqiang Xu, Hanwen Xu, Pengrui Han, Dylan Zhang, Jiashuo Sun, Chaoqi Yang, Kun Qian, Tian Wang, Changran Hu, Manling Li, Quanzheng Li, Hao Peng, Sheng Wang, Jingbo Shang, Chao Zhang, Jiaxuan You, Liyuan Liu, Pan Lu, Yu Zhang, Heng Ji, Yejin Choi, Dawn Song, Jimeng Sun, Jiawei Han
First: 2025-12-18T08:38:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T07:39:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents are moving beyond prompting alone. ChatGPT marked the rise of general-purpose LLM assistants, DeepSeek showed that on-policy reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards can improve reasoning and tool use, and OpenClaw highlights a newer direction in which agents accumulate persistent memory and reusable skills. Yet the research landscape remains fragmented across post-training, retrieval, memory, and skill systems. This survey studies these developments under a single notion of \emph{adaptation}: improving an agent, its tools, or their interaction after pretraining. We organize the field with a four-paradigm framework spanning agent adaptation and tool adaptation. On the agent side, A1 (tool-execution-signaled) and A2 (agent-output-signaled) improve the agent itself through supervised fine-tuning, preference optimization, and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. On the tool side, T1 (agent-agnostic) provides reusable pre-trained modules any agent can call, while T2 (agent-supervised) uses the agent's outputs to train memory systems, skill libraries, or lightweight subagents. Using this framework, we review post-training methods, adaptive memory architectures, and agent skills; compare their trade-offs in cost, flexibility, and generalization; and summarize evaluation practices across deep research, software development, computer use, and drug discovery. We conclude by outlining open problems in agent-tool co-adaptation, continual learning, safety, and efficient deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：智能体AI的适应机制：训练后优化、记忆与技能综述
大语言模型（LLM）智能体正超越单纯提示的范畴。ChatGPT标志着通用LLM助手的崛起，DeepSeek展示了基于可验证奖励的同策略强化学习如何提升推理与工具使用能力，而OpenClaw则凸显了智能体积累持久记忆与可复用技能的新方向。然而，当前研究在训练后优化、检索、记忆与技能系统领域仍呈碎片化。本综述将这些进展统一纳入“适应”概念框架下研究：即在预训练后改进智能体、其工具或二者交互。我们通过涵盖智能体适应与工具适应的四范式框架梳理该领域：在智能体侧，A1（工具执行信号驱动）与A2（智能体输出信号驱动）通过监督微调、偏好优化及可验证奖励强化学习改进智能体本身；在工具侧，T1（智能体无关型）提供任何智能体均可调用的预训练模块，T2（智能体监督型）则利用智能体输出训练记忆系统、技能库或轻量子智能体。基于此框架，我们系统回顾训练后优化方法、自适应记忆架构与智能体技能；比较其在成本、灵活性与泛化能力上的权衡；并总结深度学习研究、软件开发、计算机操作与药物发现等领域的评估实践。最后，我们展望智能体-工具协同适应、持续学习、安全性与高效部署等开放性问题。
Summary / 总结
This survey addresses the fragmented research landscape in adapting large language model (LLM) agents beyond initial pretraining, motivated by the need to systematically improve agent capabilities, tools, and their interaction post-deployment. It proposes a unifying framework of adaptation organized into four paradigms: two for agent adaptation (A1 and A2, using signals from tool execution or agent outputs to guide fine-tuning, preference optimization, or reinforcement learning) and two for tool adaptation (T1 and T2, involving reusable pre-trained modules or agent-supervised training of memory systems and skill libraries). The main experimental results reviewed highlight that methods like on-policy reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards enhance reasoning and tool use, while adaptive memory and skill systems improve performance across domains such as software development, computer use, and drug discovery, though trade-offs in cost, flexibility, and generalization persist.
本综述针对大语言模型（LLM）智能体在初始预训练后适应能力研究碎片化的问题，旨在系统性地提升智能体能力、工具及其交互。它提出了一个统一的适应框架，包含四种范式：两种用于智能体适应（A1和A2，利用工具执行或智能体输出的信号指导微调、偏好优化或强化学习），两种用于工具适应（T1和T2，涉及可重用的预训练模块或基于智能体输出的记忆系统和技能库训练）。回顾的主要实验结果表明，采用可验证奖励的策略强化学习等方法能增强推理和工具使用能力，而自适应记忆和技能系统在软件开发、计算机使用和药物发现等领域提升了性能，但成本、灵活性和泛化性方面的权衡依然存在。
Thickening-to-Thinning: Reward Shaping via Human-Inspired Learning Dynamics for LLM Reasoning
Authors: Wenze Lin, Zhen Yang, Xitai Jiang, Pony Ma, Gao Huang
First: 2026-02-04T06:55:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T07:28:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a promising paradigm for enhancing reasoning in Large Language Models (LLMs). However, it frequently encounters challenges such as entropy collapse, excessive verbosity, and insufficient exploration for hard problems. Crucially, existing reward schemes fail to distinguish between the need for extensive search during problem-solving and the efficiency required for mastered knowledge. In this work, we introduce T2T(Thickening-to-Thinning), a dynamic reward framework inspired by human learning processes. Specifically, it implements a dual-phase mechanism: (1) On incorrect attempts, T2T incentivizes "thickening" (longer trajectories) to broaden the search space and explore novel solution paths; (2) Upon achieving correctness, it shifts to "thinning", imposing length penalties to discourage redundancy, thereby fostering model confidence and crystallizing reasoning capabilities. Extensive experiments on mathematical benchmarks (MATH-500, AIME, AMC) across Qwen-series and Deepseek models demonstrate that T2T significantly outperforms standard GRPO and recent baselines, achieving superior performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从增厚到精简：基于人类学习动态的奖励塑形机制用于大语言模型推理
可验证奖励强化学习已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的重要范式，但常面临熵崩溃、表达冗余及难题探索不足等挑战。现有奖励机制未能区分问题求解所需的广泛搜索与已掌握知识的高效运用。本研究提出受人类学习过程启发的动态奖励框架T2T，其采用双阶段机制：(1) 错误尝试时激励“增厚”以扩展搜索空间并探索新解路径；(2) 获得正确答案后转为“精简”，通过长度惩罚减少冗余以增强模型置信度并固化推理能力。在Qwen系列和Deepseek模型上的数学基准测试表明，T2T显著优于标准GRPO及近期基线方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses limitations in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for enhancing LLM reasoning, such as entropy collapse and insufficient exploration, by proposing a dynamic reward framework called T2T (Thickening-to-Thinning) inspired by human learning. The method employs a dual-phase mechanism: during incorrect attempts, it rewards longer reasoning trajectories ('thickening') to encourage broader exploration, and upon correct solutions, it penalizes excessive length ('thinning') to promote efficiency and consolidate knowledge. Experimental results on mathematical benchmarks like MATH-500 show that T2T significantly outperforms standard GRPO and other baselines across models such as Qwen and Deepseek, achieving superior reasoning performance.
本文针对使用可验证奖励的强化学习在提升大语言模型推理能力时遇到的熵崩溃和探索不足等局限，提出了一种受人类学习启发的动态奖励框架T2T（由厚到薄）。该方法采用双阶段机制：在错误尝试时奖励更长的推理轨迹（'增厚'）以鼓励广泛探索，而在获得正确答案后则惩罚冗余长度（'减薄'）以提升效率并巩固知识。在MATH-500等数学基准上的实验结果表明，T2T在Qwen和Deepseek等模型上显著优于标准的GRPO及近期基线，实现了更优的推理性能。
More Women, Same Stereotypes: Unpacking the Gender Bias Paradox in Large Language Models
Authors: Evan Chen, Run-Jun Zhan, Yan-Bai Lin, Hung-Hsuan Chen
First: 2025-03-20T07:15:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T06:46:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have revolutionized natural language processing, yet concerns persist regarding their tendency to reflect or amplify social biases. This study introduces a novel evaluation framework to uncover gender biases in LLMs: using free-form storytelling to surface biases embedded within the models. A systematic analysis of ten prominent LLMs shows a consistent pattern of overrepresenting female characters across occupations, likely due to supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF). Paradoxically, despite this overrepresentation, the occupational gender distributions produced by these LLMs align more closely with human stereotypes than with real-world labor data. This highlights the challenge and importance of implementing balanced mitigation measures to promote fairness and prevent the establishment of potentially new biases. We release the prompts and LLM-generated stories at GitHub.
中文标题/摘要
标题：女性角色增多，刻板印象依旧：解构大语言模型中的性别偏见悖论
大语言模型（LLMs）虽已革新自然语言处理领域，但其反映或放大社会偏见的倾向仍受持续关注。本研究引入一种新颖的评估框架，通过自由叙事任务揭示LLMs中嵌入的性别偏见。对十个主流LLMs的系统分析显示：由于监督微调（SFT）和人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）的影响，模型普遍存在女性职业角色过度表征现象。然而悖论在于，尽管存在过度表征，这些LLMs生成的职业性别分布却更接近人类刻板印象而非现实劳动力数据。这凸显了实施平衡缓解措施以促进公平、防止潜在新偏见形成的重要挑战。相关提示词与LLM生成故事已发布于GitHub。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by concerns that large language models (LLMs) may reflect or amplify social biases, this study introduces a novel evaluation framework using free-form storytelling to surface embedded gender biases. The method involves a systematic analysis of ten prominent LLMs, revealing that supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning from human feedback lead to a consistent overrepresentation of female characters across occupations. Paradoxically, the main experimental result shows that despite this overrepresentation, the occupational gender distributions generated by the models align more closely with human stereotypes than with real-world labor data, underscoring the need for balanced mitigation measures to prevent new biases.
本研究针对大型语言模型可能反映或放大社会偏见的担忧，引入了一种新颖的评估框架，利用自由形式的故事生成来揭示模型中嵌入的性别偏见。方法上，通过对十个主流模型的系统分析，发现监督微调和基于人类反馈的强化学习导致了女性角色在职业描述中的持续过度表征。主要的实验结果揭示了一个悖论：尽管存在这种过度表征，模型生成的职业性别分布却更接近人类刻板印象而非现实劳动力数据，这凸显了实施平衡的缓解措施以防止新偏见产生的重要性和挑战。
MJ1: Multimodal Judgment via Grounded Verification
Authors: Bhavesh Kumar, Dylan Feng, Leonard Tang
First: 2026-03-09T05:55:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:55:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal judges struggle to ground decisions in visual evidence. We present MJ1, a multimodal judge trained with reinforcement learning that enforces visual grounding through a structured grounded verification chain (observations $\rightarrow$ claims $\rightarrow$ verification $\rightarrow$ evaluation $\rightarrow$ scoring) and a counterfactual consistency reward that penalizes position bias. Even without training, our mechanism improves base-model accuracy on MMRB2 by +3.8 points on Image Editing and +1.7 on Multimodal Reasoning. After training, MJ1, with only 3B active parameters, achieves 77.0% accuracy on MMRB2 and surpasses orders-of-magnitude larger models like Gemini-3-Pro. These results show that grounded verification and consistency-based training substantially improve multimodal judgment without increasing model scale.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MJ1：基于视觉验证的多模态判断模型
多模态判断模型难以将决策基于视觉证据。我们提出MJ1，一种通过强化学习训练的多模态判断模型，采用结构化视觉验证链（观察→主张→验证→评估→评分）强制实现视觉验证，并通过反事实一致性奖励机制惩罚立场偏差。即使未经训练，该机制在MMRB2基准上使基础模型在图像编辑任务准确率提升3.8个百分点，多模态推理任务提升1.7个百分点。训练后，仅含30亿激活参数的MJ1在MMRB2上达到77.0%准确率，超越Gemini-3-Pro等规模大数个数量级的模型。结果表明，视觉验证与基于一致性的训练能显著提升多模态判断能力，且无需扩大模型规模。

The paper addresses the issue that multimodal judges often fail to ground their decisions in visual evidence. Experimentally, even before training, this mechanism boosts base-model accuracy on the MMRB2 benchmark by +3.8 points in Image Editing and +1.7 in Multimodal Reasoning. After training, MJ1, with only 3 billion active parameters, achieves 77.0% accuracy on MMRB2, outperforming much larger models like Gemini-3-Pro, demonstrating that grounded verification and consistency-based training significantly enhance multimodal judgment without scaling model size.
