A Simple "Motivation" Can Enhance Reinforcement Finetuning of Large Reasoning Models
Authors: Junjie Zhang, Guozheng Ma, Shunyu Liu, Haoyu Wang, Jiaxing Huang, Ting-En Lin, Fei Huang, Yongbin Li, Dacheng Tao
First: 2025-06-23T10:37:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:26:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards~(RLVR) has emerged as a powerful learn-to-reason paradigm for large reasoning models to tackle complex tasks. However, the current RLVR paradigm is still not efficient enough, as it works in a trial-and-error manner. To perform better, the model needs to explore the reward space by numerously generating responses and learn from fragmented reward signals, blind to the overall reward patterns. Fortunately, verifiable rewards make the natural language description of the reward function possible, and meanwhile, LLMs have demonstrated strong in-context learning ability. This motivates us to explore if large reasoning models can benefit from a \textbf{motivation} of the task, \textit{i.e.}, awareness of the reward function, during the reinforcement finetuning process, as we humans sometimes do when learning. In this paper, we introduce \textit{\textbf{M}otivation-\textbf{e}nhanced \textbf{R}einforcement \textbf{F}inetuning}~(\textbf{MeRF}), an intuitive yet effective method enhancing reinforcement finetuning of LLMs by involving \emph{``telling LLMs rules of the game''}. Specifically, \textbf{MeRF} directly injects the reward specification into the prompt, which serves as an in-context motivation for the model to be aware of the optimization objective. This simple modification leverages the in-context learning ability of LLMs, aligning generation with optimization, thereby incentivizing the model to generate desired outputs from both inner motivation and external reward. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that \textbf{MeRF} achieves substantial performance gains over the RLVR baseline. Moreover, ablation studies show that MeRF performs better with greater consistency between the in-context motivation and the external reward function, while the model also demonstrates an ability to adapt to misleading motivations through reinforcement finetuning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：简单“动机”可增强大型推理模型的强化微调
可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为大型推理模型处理复杂任务的强大学习推理范式。然而，当前RLVR范式仍不够高效，因其以试错方式运作。为提升性能，模型需通过大量生成响应来探索奖励空间，并从零散的奖励信号中学习，却无法把握整体奖励模式。幸运的是，可验证奖励使奖励函数的自然语言描述成为可能，同时大语言模型展现出强大的上下文学习能力。这促使我们探索：在强化微调过程中，大型推理模型能否像人类学习时那样，从任务的\textbf{动机}（即对奖励函数的认知）中获益。本文提出\textbf{动机增强强化微调}（\textbf{MeRF}），这是一种通过\emph{“告知大语言模型规则”}来增强大语言模型强化微调的直观有效方法。具体而言，\textbf{MeRF}将奖励规范直接注入提示词，作为模型的上下文动机，使其认知优化目标。这一简单改进利用了大语言模型的上下文学习能力，使生成与优化对齐，从而激励模型同时基于内在动机和外部奖励生成期望输出。实证评估表明，\textbf{MeRF}较RLVR基线取得显著性能提升。此外，消融研究显示，当上下文动机与外部奖励函数更一致时，MeRF表现更优，同时模型也展现出通过强化微调适应误导性动机的能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the inefficiency of current Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods, which rely on trial-and-error exploration without awareness of the overall reward function. To address this, the authors propose MeRF, a method that enhances reinforcement finetuning by directly injecting a natural language description of the reward specification into the prompt, serving as an in-context motivation for the model to align its generation with the optimization objective. Experimental results show that MeRF achieves substantial performance gains over the RLVR baseline, with ablation studies indicating better performance when the motivation aligns with the reward function and an ability to adapt to misleading motivations through finetuning.
本文的动机在于当前基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方法效率不足，其以试错方式运行，模型缺乏对整体奖励模式的认知。为此，作者提出了MeRF方法，通过将奖励规则的自然语言描述直接注入提示中，作为上下文动机，使模型在强化微调过程中能意识到优化目标，从而利用大语言模型的上下文学习能力来对齐生成与优化。实验结果表明，MeRF相比RLVR基线取得了显著的性能提升，消融研究显示当动机与奖励函数一致时效果更好，同时模型也展现出通过强化微调适应误导性动机的能力。
VORL-EXPLORE: A Hybrid Learning Planning Approach to Multi-Robot Exploration in Dynamic Environments
Authors: Ning Liu, Sen Shen, Zheng Li, Sheng Liu, Dongkun Han, Shangke Lyu, Thomas Braunl
First: 2026-03-09T05:20:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:20:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hierarchical multi-robot exploration commonly decouples frontier allocation from local navigation, which can make the system brittle in dense and dynamic environments. Because the allocator lacks direct awareness of execution difficulty, robots may cluster at bottlenecks, trigger oscillatory replanning, and generate redundant coverage. We propose VORL-EXPLORE, a hybrid learning and planning framework that addresses this limitation through execution fidelity, a shared estimate of local navigability that couples task allocation with motion execution. This fidelity signal is incorporated into a fidelity-coupled Voronoi objective with inter-robot repulsion to reduce contention before it emerges. It also drives a risk-aware adaptive arbitration mechanism between global A* guidance and a reactive reinforcement learning policy, balancing long-range efficiency with safe interaction in confined spaces. The framework further supports online self-supervised recalibration of the fidelity model using pseudo-labels derived from recent progress and safety outcomes, enabling adaptation to non-stationary obstacles without manual risk tuning. We evaluate this capability separately in a dedicated severe-traffic ablation. Extensive experiments in randomized grids and a Gazebo factory scenario show high success rates, shorter path length, lower overlap, and robust collision avoidance. The source code will be made publicly available upon acceptance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VORL-EXPLORE：动态环境中多机器人探索的混合学习规划方法
传统分层多机器人探索常将边界分配与局部导航解耦，在密集动态环境中易导致系统脆弱。由于分配器缺乏对执行难度的直接感知，机器人可能聚集于瓶颈区域，引发振荡重规划并产生冗余覆盖。本文提出VORL-EXPLORE混合学习规划框架，通过引入'执行保真度'——耦合任务分配与运动执行的局部可通行性共享估计——解决该局限。该保真度信号融入具有机器人间斥力的保真耦合Voronoi目标函数，以预先消解冲突；同时驱动全局A*引导与反应式强化学习策略间的风险感知自适应仲裁机制，在狭窄空间中平衡长程效率与安全交互。框架进一步支持基于近期进展与安全结果生成的伪标签，对保真度模型进行在线自监督重校准，无需人工风险调参即可适应非稳态障碍物。该能力在专项密集交通消融实验中独立验证。随机栅格与Gazebo工厂场景的大量实验表明，本方法在成功率、路径长度、覆盖重叠度与碰撞避免方面均表现优异。源代码将在论文录用后公开。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the brittleness of hierarchical multi-robot exploration in dense, dynamic environments, where decoupled allocation and navigation cause clustering and inefficiency. The method, VORL-EXPLORE, introduces a hybrid learning and planning framework that uses a shared execution fidelity signal to couple task allocation with motion execution; this signal informs a fidelity-coupled Voronoi objective for allocation and an adaptive arbitration mechanism between global A* planning and a reactive RL policy for navigation, with online self-supervised recalibration of the fidelity model. Experimental results in randomized grids and a Gazebo factory scenario demonstrate high success rates, shorter path lengths, reduced overlap, and robust collision avoidance, with a separate ablation confirming adaptation to severe traffic.
本文的动机是解决密集动态环境中分层多机器人探索的脆弱性问题，其中解耦的任务分配与导航会导致机器人聚集和效率低下。所提出的VORL-EXPLORE方法是一种混合学习与规划框架，它通过共享的执行保真度信号将任务分配与运动执行耦合；该信号用于指导保真度耦合的Voronoi目标分配，以及全局A*规划与反应式强化学习策略之间的自适应仲裁导航机制，并支持基于伪标签的在线自监督保真度模型重新校准。在随机网格和Gazebo工厂场景中的大量实验结果表明，该方法实现了高成功率、更短路径长度、更低重叠率和鲁棒的碰撞避免，一项专门的严重交通消融实验也验证了其对非平稳障碍物的适应能力。
Advancing Automated Algorithm Design via Evolutionary Stagewise Design with LLMs
Authors: Chen Lu, Ke Xue, Chengrui Gao, Yunqi Shi, Siyuan Xu, Mingxuan Yuan, Chao Qian, Zhi-Hua Zhou
First: 2026-03-09T05:13:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:13:44+00:00
Comments: 28 pages, 19 figures and 7 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the rapid advancement of human science and technology, problems in industrial scenarios are becoming increasingly challenging, bringing significant challenges to traditional algorithm design. Automated algorithm design with LLMs emerges as a promising solution, but the currently adopted black-box modeling deprives LLMs of any awareness of the intrinsic mechanism of the target problem, leading to hallucinated designs. In this paper, we introduce Evolutionary Stagewise Algorithm Design (EvoStage), a novel evolutionary paradigm that bridges the gap between the rigorous demands of industrial-scale algorithm design and the LLM-based algorithm design methods. Drawing inspiration from CoT, EvoStage decomposes the algorithm design process into sequential, manageable stages and integrates real-time intermediate feedback to iteratively refine algorithm design directions. To further reduce the algorithm design space and avoid falling into local optima, we introduce a multi-agent system and a "global-local perspective" mechanism. We apply EvoStage to the design of two types of common optimizers: designing parameter configuration schedules of the Adam optimizer for chip placement, and designing acquisition functions of Bayesian optimization for black-box optimization. Experimental results across open-source benchmarks demonstrate that EvoStage outperforms human-expert designs and existing LLM-based methods within only a couple of evolution steps, even achieving the historically state-of-the-art half-perimeter wire-length results on every tested chip case. Furthermore, when deployed on a commercial-grade 3D chip placement tool, EvoStage significantly surpasses the original performance metrics, achieving record-breaking efficiency. We hope EvoStage can significantly advance automated algorithm design in the real world, helping elevate human productivity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于LLM的进化分阶段设计推进自动化算法设计
随着人类科学技术的飞速发展，工业场景中的问题日益复杂，给传统算法设计带来巨大挑战。基于大语言模型（LLM）的自动化算法设计成为一种有前景的解决方案，但当前采用的黑箱建模使LLM无法感知目标问题的内在机制，导致设计结果存在幻觉。本文提出进化分阶段算法设计（EvoStage），这是一种新颖的进化范式，旨在弥合工业级算法设计的严谨需求与基于LLM的算法设计方法之间的差距。受思维链（CoT）启发，EvoStage将算法设计过程分解为连续可控的阶段，并通过实时中间反馈迭代优化算法设计方向。为减少算法设计空间并避免陷入局部最优，我们引入了多智能体系统和“全局-局部视角”机制。我们将EvoStage应用于两类常见优化器的设计：为芯片布局设计Adam优化器的参数配置方案，以及为黑盒优化设计贝叶斯优化的采集函数。在开源基准测试上的实验结果表明，EvoStage仅需少数进化步骤即可超越人类专家设计和现有基于LLM的方法，甚至在所有测试芯片案例中均实现了历史最优的半周长线长结果。此外，在商用级3D芯片布局工具中部署时，EvoStage显著超越了原始性能指标，实现了破纪录的效率。我们希望EvoStage能切实推动现实世界中的自动化算法设计，助力提升人类生产效率。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of black-box LLM-based automated algorithm design, which lacks awareness of problem mechanisms and leads to hallucinated outputs, this paper introduces Evolutionary Stagewise Algorithm Design (EvoStage). The method decomposes algorithm design into sequential stages with real-time feedback, incorporating a multi-agent system and a global-local perspective to refine designs and avoid local optima. Experimental results on designing Adam optimizer schedules for chip placement and acquisition functions for Bayesian optimization show that EvoStage outperforms human experts and existing LLM methods within few evolution steps, achieving state-of-the-art wire-length results on chip cases and record-breaking efficiency in a commercial 3D placement tool.
针对现有基于大语言模型的自动化算法设计采用黑箱建模、缺乏对问题内在机制的认知而导致幻觉设计的问题，本文提出了进化分阶段算法设计方法。该方法受思维链启发，将算法设计分解为可管理的顺序阶段，并融入实时反馈进行迭代优化，同时引入多智能体系统和“全局-局部视角”机制以减少搜索空间并避免局部最优。在芯片布局的Adam优化器参数配置设计和贝叶斯优化采集函数设计的实验中，该方法仅需少量进化步骤即超越人类专家设计和现有基于大语言模型的方法，在所有测试芯片案例上取得了历史最优的半周长线长结果，并在商用三维芯片布局工具中实现了破纪录的效率提升。
Reinforcement Learning for Individual Optimal Policy from Heterogeneous Data
Authors: Rui Miao, Babak Shahbaba, Annie Qu
First: 2025-05-14T15:44:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:07:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline reinforcement learning (RL) aims to find optimal policies in dynamic environments in order to maximize the expected total rewards by leveraging pre-collected data. Learning from heterogeneous data is one of the fundamental challenges in offline RL. Traditional methods focus on learning an optimal policy for all individuals with pre-collected data from a single episode or homogeneous batch episodes, and thus, may result in a suboptimal policy for a heterogeneous population. In this paper, we propose an individualized offline policy optimization framework for heterogeneous time-stationary Markov decision processes (MDPs). The proposed heterogeneous model with individual latent variables enables us to efficiently estimate the individual Q-functions, and our Penalized Pessimistic Personalized Policy Learning (P4L) algorithm guarantees a fast rate on the average regret under a weak partial coverage assumption on behavior policies. In addition, our simulation studies and a real data application demonstrate the superior numerical performance of the proposed method compared with existing methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于异构数据的个体最优策略强化学习
离线强化学习旨在利用预先收集的数据，在动态环境中寻找最优策略以最大化期望总奖励。从异构数据中学习是离线强化学习的核心挑战之一。传统方法侧重于利用单次或同质批次收集的数据为所有个体学习统一最优策略，这可能导致对异质群体产生次优策略。本文针对异质时间平稳马尔可夫决策过程，提出了一种个体化离线策略优化框架。该包含个体隐变量的异质模型能有效估计个体Q函数，我们提出的惩罚悲观个性化策略学习算法在行为策略弱部分覆盖假设下，可保证平均遗憾的快速收敛速率。仿真研究与实际数据应用表明，所提方法较现有方法具有更优越的数值性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of learning optimal policies from heterogeneous offline data, where traditional methods that assume homogeneity can yield suboptimal results for diverse individuals. The authors propose an individualized offline policy optimization framework for heterogeneous time-stationary Markov decision processes, incorporating individual latent variables to estimate Q-functions efficiently, and introduce the Penalized Pessimistic Personalized Policy Learning (P4L) algorithm, which ensures a fast regret rate under weak partial coverage assumptions. Experimental results from simulations and a real-world application show that this method outperforms existing approaches in numerical performance.
本文针对从异构离线数据中学习最优策略的挑战，传统方法假设同质性可能导致对多样化个体产生次优策略。作者提出了一个针对异构时间平稳马尔可夫决策过程的个性化离线策略优化框架，通过引入个体潜变量来高效估计Q函数，并提出了惩罚悲观个性化策略学习（P4L）算法，该算法在弱部分覆盖假设下保证了较快的遗憾率。仿真研究和实际数据应用表明，该方法在数值性能上优于现有方法。
Local Constrained Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Jing Jingzhe, Fan Zheyi, Szu Hui Ng, Qingpei Hu
First: 2026-03-09T05:05:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T05:05:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimization (BO) for high-dimensional constrained problems remains a significant challenge due to the curse of dimensionality. We propose Local Constrained Bayesian Optimization (LCBO), a novel framework tailored for such settings. Unlike trust-region methods that are prone to premature shrinking when confronting tight or complex constraints, LCBO leverages the differentiable landscape of constraint-penalized surrogates to alternate between rapid local descent and uncertainty-driven exploration. Theoretically, we prove that LCBO achieves a convergence rate for the Karush-Kuhn-Tucker (KKT) residual that depends polynomially on the dimension $d$ for common kernels under mild assumptions, offering a rigorous alternative to global BO where regret bounds typically scale exponentially. Extensive evaluations on high-dimensional benchmarks (up to 100D) demonstrate that LCBO consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：局部约束贝叶斯优化
高维约束问题的贝叶斯优化（BO）因维度灾难而面临重大挑战。本文提出适用于此类场景的新型框架——局部约束贝叶斯优化（LCBO）。与面对严格或复杂约束时易过早收缩的置信域方法不同，LCBO利用约束惩罚代理模型的可微分特性，在快速局部下降与不确定性驱动探索间交替进行。理论上，我们证明在温和假设下，LCBO对常见核函数获得的KKT残差收敛速率与维度$d$呈多项式关系，为通常具有指数级遗憾界的全局BO提供了严格替代方案。在高维基准测试（最高100维）上的广泛评估表明，LCBO持续优于最先进的基线方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of performing Bayesian optimization (BO) in high-dimensional constrained settings, where traditional methods struggle with the curse of dimensionality. The authors propose Local Constrained Bayesian Optimization (LCBO), a framework that uses differentiable constraint-penalized surrogate models to alternate between fast local descent and exploration guided by uncertainty, avoiding issues like premature shrinking seen in trust-region approaches. Theoretically, LCBO achieves a polynomial convergence rate for the KKT residual with respect to dimension under mild assumptions, contrasting with the exponential scaling in global BO regret bounds. Experimental results on benchmarks up to 100 dimensions show that LCBO consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baseline methods.
本文针对高维约束场景下的贝叶斯优化难题，传统方法因维度诅咒而效果受限。作者提出了局部约束贝叶斯优化（LCBO）框架，该方法利用可微的约束惩罚代理模型，在快速局部下降和不确定性驱动的探索之间交替进行，避免了信任域方法中常见的过早收缩问题。理论上，在温和假设下，LCBO对KKT残差实现了关于维度的多项式收敛速率，这与全局贝叶斯优化中遗憾界限通常呈指数缩放形成对比。在高达100维的基准测试中，实验结果表明LCBO持续优于现有先进基线方法。
RL unknotter, hard unknots and unknotting number
Authors: Anne Dranowski, Yura Kabkov, Daniel Tubbenhauer
First: 2026-03-09T04:43:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-09T04:43:59+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, many figures, comments welcome
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We develop a reinforcement learning pipeline for simplifying knot diagrams. A trained agent learns move proposals and a value heuristic for navigating Reidemeister moves. The pipeline applies to arbitrary knots and links; we test it on ``very hard'' unknot diagrams and, using diagram inflation, on $4_1\#9_{10}$ where we recover the recently established and surprising upper bound of three for the unknotting number.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习解结器、困难解结与解结数
我们开发了一种用于简化纽结图的强化学习流程。训练后的智能体学习移动提议和用于导航Reidemeister移动的价值启发式方法。该流程适用于任意纽结与链环；我们在“极难”解结图上进行测试，并通过图膨胀技术应用于$4_1\#9_{10}$纽结，成功恢复了近期确立且令人惊讶的解结数上界——三。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of simplifying complex knot diagrams, this paper introduces a reinforcement learning pipeline that trains an agent to propose and evaluate Reidemeister moves. The method is general for arbitrary knots and links, and its experimental application to 'very hard' unknot diagrams and the composite knot 4_1#9_10 successfully recovers the known unknotting number upper bound of three, demonstrating the pipeline's effectiveness.
本文旨在简化复杂的纽结图，提出了一种强化学习流程，训练智能体来提议和评估Reidemeister移动。该方法适用于任意纽结和链环，实验应用于“极难”解结图及复合纽结4_1#9_10，成功恢复了已知的解结数上界为三的结果，验证了该流程的有效性。
